The diagram depicts interactions between several entities: UE (User Equipment), 5G-L1-UL, 5G-L1-DL, 5G-L2-PS, 5G-L2-LO, 5G-L2-HI DU, and 5G C-Plane. The sequence of events is as follows: 1. UL HARQ Tx. See MSC 5G_L1L2_FLOW_562 : This indicates an uplink HARQ transmission from the UE, referencing a specific message flow. 2. LoCtrl_UIMacPduReceiveInd : A control message is received by the 5G-L2-LO entity. 3. LoData_UIRIcPduReceiveInd : Data is received by the 5G-L2-LO entity. 4. HiSgnIDu_SrbReceiveInd : A signal is received by the 5G-L2-HI DU entity. 5. RLC acknowledgement (DL data on DCCH in gNB-DU). See MSC 5G_L1L2_FLOW_252 : An RLC acknowledgement is sent, indicating the reception of downlink data on DCCH in the gNB-DU, referencing another message flow. 6. UL RRC message transfer over F1-C interface. Not visible to U-Plane : This box, connected by a dashed arrow from the RLC acknowledgement, describes the transfer of an UL RRC message over the F1-C interface, which is not visible to the U-Plane. 7. Below the RLC acknowledgement, there is a dotted box listing three SRB (Signaling Radio Bearer) identifiers with their types: * [5GC000723-A] SRB1 (SA) * [5GC000752-A] SRB2 (SA) * [5GC000578-D] SRB3 (NSA) The title of the diagram is "MSC.15322 UL data on DCCH in gNB-DU".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_3281.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to the drawing: (ID: 11200425)

(RLC AM) [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating UL (Uplink) user data transmission in a 5G network, specifically focusing on DTCH (Dedicated Control Channel) with RLC AM (Radio Link Control - Acknowledged Mode). The diagram depicts interactions between several network entities: - UE (User Equipment) - 5G-L1-UL (5G Layer 1 - Uplink) - 5G-L1-DL (5G Layer 1 - Downlink) - 5G-L2-PS (5G Layer 2 - Packet Switched) - 5G-L2-LO (5G Layer 2 - Logical Operations) - 5G-L2-HI DU (5G Layer 2 - High Interface, Distributed Unit) - 5G-L2-HI CU (5G Layer 2 - High Interface, Centralized Unit) - 5G C-Plane (5G Control Plane) - S-GW / NG-U (Serving Gateway / Next Generation User Plane) - MeNB (Master eNodeB) The diagram shows the following sequence of events and messages: 1. UL HARQ Tx. See MSC 5G_L1L2_FLOW_562 : This indicates the transmission of Uplink Hybrid Automatic Repeat Request (HARQ) from the UE. 2. LoCtr_UIMacPduReceiveInd : A control indication received by the 5G-L2-LO entity. 3. LoData_UIRIcPduReceiveInd (User data RLC control PDU) : A data indication, specifically a User Data RLC Control Protocol Data Unit, received by the 5G-L2-LO entity. 4. par : This label likely signifies a parallel execution or a grouping of related actions. 5. RLC acknowledgement (DL data on DL-SCH). See MSC 5G_L1L2_FLOW_255 : An RLC acknowledgement message related to Downlink data on the Downlink Shared Channel. 6. GTP-U PDU (RLC SDU) : A GTP-U (GPRS Tunneling Protocol - User Plane) Protocol Data Unit, carrying an RLC Service Data Unit, is sent from the 5G-L2-HI CU to the S-GW / NG-U. 7. PDCP COUNT Rollover indication: 3GPP NSA [5GC000866-H] 3GPP SA : This is an optional indication related to PDCP (Packet Data Convergence Protocol) COUNT rollover, specific to 3GPP NSA (Non-Standalone) mode. 8. opt HiUserCu_PdcpMaxCountind : An optional message, "HiUserCu_PdcpMaxCountind", is sent from the 5G-L2-HI CU. 9. GTP-U PDU (PDCP SDU) : A GTP-U PDU carrying a PDCP SDU is sent from the 5G-L2-HI CU to the S-GW / NG-U. 10. 5G-L2-HI receives RLC SDU from eNB and sends PDCP SDU to S-GW (NSA only) : This is a descriptive box indicating that the 5G-L2-HI entity receives an RLC SDU from the eNB (evolved NodeB) and forwards a PDCP SDU to the S-GW, specifically in NSA mode. 11. opt GTP-U PDU (RLC SDU) : Another optional GTP-U PDU carrying an RLC SDU is sent. 12. opt GTP-U PDU (PDCP SDU) : Another optional GTP-U PDU carrying a PDCP SDU is sent. 13. MeNB is valid for NSA only : A note indicating that the MeNB entity is relevant only for NSA deployments. The diagram visually represents the flow of data and control messages between different layers and network functions during uplink user data transmission in a 5G RLC AM scenario.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_3287.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to the drawing: (ID: 11200485)

It depicts the interaction between different network functions within a gNB-MN (gNB-Mobility Anchor) and a gNB-SN (gNB-Split Node). The participants in the diagram are: - gNB-MN : - 5G-L2-PS (Physical Layer - PS) - 5G-L2-LO (Lower Layer - LO) - 5G-L2-HI (DU) (Higher Layer - DU) - gNB-SN : - 5G-L2-HI (CU) (Higher Layer - CU) - 5G-CP (Control Plane) - UPF (User Plane Function) The sequence of events is as follows: 1. 5G-L2-PS sends a LoCtrl_UIMacPduReceiveInd message to 5G-L2-LO . 2. 5G-L2-LO sends a LoData_UIRIcPduReceiveInd message, containing "RLC User data / control PDU", to 5G-L2-HI (DU) . 3. 5G-L2-HI (DU) sends a GTP-U PDU message, described as "RLC SDU over Xn-U tunnel", to 5G-L2-HI (CU) . 4. A diamond-shaped box indicates an event: PDCP COUNT Rollover detected . This event is associated with the interaction between 5G-L2-HI (CU) and 5G-CP . 5. 5G-L2-HI (CU) sends a HiUserCu_PdcpMaxCountInd message to 5G-CP . 6. 5G-CP sends a GTP-U PDU message, containing "PDCP SDU", to UPF . The diagram uses dashed boxes to group the components belonging to gNB-MN and gNB-SN. The "Opt" label near the message from 5G-L2-HI (DU) to 5G-L2-HI (CU) suggests an optional path or condition.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_3290.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to the "5G_L1L2_FLOW_4624_UL_data_on_DTCH_RLC_AM_over_Xn_Interface.signalling" file: (ID: 11200511)

The diagram shows interactions between several network entities: UE (User Equipment), 5G-L1-UL (5G Layer 1 Uplink), 5G-L1-DL (5G Layer 1 Downlink), 5G-L2-PS (5G Layer 2 Packet Switched), 5G-L2-LO (5G Layer 2 Lower), 5G-L2-HI DU (5G Layer 2 High-layer DU - Distributed Unit), 5G-L2-HI CU (5G Layer 2 High-layer CU - Centralized Unit), and S-GW / NG-U (Serving Gateway / Next-Generation User Plane). The diagram depicts the following sequence of events: 1. UL HARQ Tx. See MSC 5G_L1L2_FLOW_562 : This indicates an uplink HARQ (Hybrid Automatic Repeat reQuest) transmission initiated by the UE, referencing a specific message flow. This message is shown to originate from the UE and span across the L1 and L2 layers. 2. LoCtr_UIMacPduReceiveInd : The 5G-L2-PS entity receives an indication from the L1 layer. 3. LoData_UIRIcPduReceiveInd (User data) : The 5G-L2-LO entity receives user data from the L2-PS entity. 4. GTP-U PDU (RLC SDU) : The 5G-L2-HI CU entity receives a GTP-U (GPRS Tunneling Protocol - User Plane) PDU, which contains an RLC SDU (Service Data Unit). 5. GTP-U PDU (PDCP SDU) : The S-GW / NG-U entity receives a GTP-U PDU, which contains a PDCP SDU (Packet Data Convergence Protocol SDU). The diagram visually represents the encapsulation and transfer of user data from the UE through various layers and network functions towards the S-GW / NG-U. The dashed box around "5G-L2-HI DU" and "5G-L2-HI CU" suggests that these two entities together form the 5G-L2-HI functional split.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_3300.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to the drawing: (ID: 11200591)

The diagram depicts interactions between different network components: UE (User Equipment), 5G-L1-UL (5G Layer 1 Uplink), 5G-L1-DL (5G Layer 1 Downlink), 5G-L2-PS (5G Layer 2 Protocol Stack), and 5G-L2-LO (5G Layer 2 Lower Layer). The diagram shows the following sequence of events: 1. Initial Transmission: * The 5G-L2-PS component sends a request message towards each 5G-L1-DL and 5G-L1-UL on a carrier allocation basis. * The 5G-L1-DL sends a DIData_PDCCHSendReq(DCI) message to the UE. * The UE responds with a PDCCH message. * The UE sends a PUSCH (TB) (Transport Block) to the 5G-L1-UL. * The 5G-L1-UL sends a UIData_PuschReceiveReq to the 5G-L1-DL. * The 5G-L1-DL sends a UIData_PuschReceiveRespPs to the 5G-L1-UL. 2. HARQ Retransmission Loop: * The diagram enters an alt (alternative) block followed by a loop block. * The loop continues until the Transport Block (TB) is correctly received OR the number of transmissions ( numOfTx ) reaches the maximum allowed ( maxUIHarqTx ). * Inside the loop, the 5G-L1-UL sends a UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU (CRC NOK) to the 5G-L2-PS, indicating a negative acknowledgment (NOK) and that the number of transmissions is less than the maximum. * The 5G-L2-PS's UL MAC Scheduling component receives this. * The 5G-L1-DL sends a DIData_PdcchSendReq(HARQ N) (UL grant &amp;&amp; NDI not toggled) to the UE. * The UE sends a PDCCH message. * The UE sends a UIData_PuschReceiveReq (receive request for ReTx) to the 5G-L1-UL. * The UE sends a PUSCH (ReTx) (retransmission) to the 5G-L1-UL. * The 5G-L1-UL sends a UIData_PuschReceiveRespPs to the 5G-L1-DL. * The 5G-L1-UL sends a UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU (CRC NOK) to the 5G-L2-PS, indicating a negative acknowledgment and that the number of transmissions has reached the maximum. 3. HARQ Release: * The 5G-L2-PS's UL MAC Scheduling component receives this. * The 5G-L2-LO component receives a UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU(CRC OK) from the 5G-L1-UL, indicating a positive acknowledgment (OK). * The 5G-L2-LO component then performs a Release HARQ operation. * The 5G-L2-LO component disassembles the TB received from each 5G-L1-UL system component on a carrier allocation basis. * The 5G-L2-LO component also notes that HARQ retransmission is done via the same 5G-L1 where the original transmission was done. * Finally, the 5G-L1-DL sends a UIData_PuschReceiveRespLo to the 5G-L2-PS. The diagram also includes annotations: * [5GC000527-A] 5G_L2-PS sends req messages toward each 5G-L1-DL and 5G-L1-UL: on carrier allocation basis. * Loop until TB is correctly received OR numOfTx reaches maxUIHarqTx * [5GC000527-A] HARQ retransmission is done via the same 5G-L1 where original transmission was done. * [5GC000527-A] 5G_L2-LO disassembles sequentially TB received from each 5G-L1-UL system component on carrier allocation basis [/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_3305.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to drawing: (ID: 11200636)

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "CFO metric handling" process within a 5G-L2-PS system. The diagram depicts interactions between different components, including L1-UL, UL Scheduler, DL Scheduler, and Cell Group.
The diagram is structured with vertical lifelines representing the components and horizontal arrows indicating messages exchanged between them. The messages are labeled with sequence numbers and descriptions.
Key elements and interactions shown in the diagram include:
\* **CFO average mode check:** The UL Scheduler initiates a check of the "CFO average mode".
\* **PUSCH handling (opt):**
\* If the CFO average mode is "PUSCH\_Only", "Both", or "Separate", a `UIData_PuschReceiveRespPs` message is sent.
\* If PUSCH reception is non-DTX, the average CFO is calculated and stored.
\* A `PsInternal_UIToDIIntraSchedUpdate` message is sent.
\* Based on whether the CFO average mode is "Separate", the calculated CFO metric is stored either in the PUSCH context or in the common context.
\* **PUCCH handling (opt):**
\* If the CFO average mode is "PUCCH\_Only", "Both", or "Separate", a `UIData_PucchReceiveRespPs` message is sent.
\* If PUCCH reception is non-DTX and Format 3, the average CFO is calculated and stored in the common context.
\* If the CFO average mode is not "Separate", a `PsInternal_DITOUIIntraSchedUpdate` message is sent, and the calculated CFO metric is stored.
\* **Parallel requests (par):**
\* `UIData_PuschReceiveReq` and `UIData_PucchReceiveReq` are sent in parallel.
The diagram also includes a footer with the text "http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v8.3.7".

[CB009169-AB] This flow is for FR1 UL CA UE SCell activation.
 
For FR1 T+F UL CA UE, no PCsi transient phase handling part (i.e. l1\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd relavant handling) because no scheduling on FDD Scell overlapping slot and no PCsi carried on Scell PUSCH. 
[End CB009169-AB]
 
 
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the SCell activation procedure in a 5G network. The diagram depicts interactions between different network functions, including gNB\_DU, PCell, and SCell.
The diagram is divided into two main sections: "1. SCell activation checking" and "2. SCell activation procedure".
**Section 1: SCell activation checking**
This section describes two cases for SCell activation:
\* **case1 UL Blind Scell activation:**
\* The UE sends `rrcReconfigCompleteReq` to the gNB\_DU.
\* This is followed by an `SCell selection` with `5G_UP_ALG_2724`.
\* **case2 UL Buffer based activation:**
\* The UE is in an "UE Inactive (SCell state in PCell)" state.
\* **(1.1) Activation condition checking:** This involves checking the buffer based on `CB006137-AB`, `5G UP ALG 9698`, and `5G_UP_ALG_9496`.
\* **(1.2) `I2_ps_internal_UITODIIntraSchedUpdate`** is sent with `SCellActivationCmdType: FR1_UIDecision_Activate_Decision`.
\* **(1.3) `SCell selection`** with `5G_UP_ALG_2724`.
**Section 2: SCell activation procedure**
This section details the steps involved in activating an SCell.
\* **ref (2.1) Activation procedure (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_290):** This is a referenced procedure.
\* **(2.2) `I2_ps_peerCtrl_PcellDpaMaxDailnd` (5G\_L2\_IF\_2210):** This message is sent from PCell to SCell.
\* **opt (2.3) PCsi transient handling:** This is an optional step.
\* `I2_ps_peerCtrl_PcsiStatusind` is sent with `Status: NOTRANSIENT` and `Cause: ACTIVE`.
\* The content includes "PCSI of Pcell and all other activated Scells".
\* A note indicates "Save PCSI to remotePcell PCSI table".
\* **(2.4) Inform Scell activation:**
\* `I2_ps_peerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq` is sent with `ModifType = START`.
\* `I2_ps_internal_DIToUlIntraSchedUpdate` is sent with `SCellActivationCmdType: FR1_Activation_ACK`.
\* `I2_ps_peerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp` is sent with `ModifType = START`.
\* **(2.5) Inform PCELL UL and start buffer split:**
\* `I2_ps_internal_DIToUlIntraSchedUpdate` is sent with `SCellActivationCmdType: FR1_Activation_ACK`.
\* This is followed by two steps: "1.Start buffer split procedure" and "2. Stop UL active checking procedure".
\* Finally, the state changes to "UE Active (SCell state in PCell)".
The diagram also shows the network functions at the top: `gNB_DU`, `PCELL_L2RT`, `PCELL_UL`, `PCELL_DL`, `SCELL_L2RT`, `SCELL_DL`, and `SCELL_UL`.
The text "UE is Pcell in service, SCell added but not activated" appears at the top, setting the context for the diagram.
The bottom right corner contains a URL: `http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v6.3.7`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3369.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
link to "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2740\_BuffBased\_Activation.signalling"

1.Scell activation checking: case 2 UL Buffer based activation checking

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201106`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
In buffer based activation mode, after reception of the PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq indicating successful SCell addition, PCell UL periodically evaluate according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9698\_replaced([11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9496\_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If activation evaluation passed, PCell UL send l2\_ps\_internal\_UlToDlIntraSchedUpdate with SCellActivationCmdType = FR1\_UlDecision\_Activate\_Decision to PCell DL. PCell DL save the decision for furthur activation checking in DL according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9771\_replaced([11120866](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
(1.1) Buffer based activation condition checking

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11201120`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
Activation condition checking is descriped in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9698\_replaced([11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9496\_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_7769\_replaced([11159027](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25OcFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_3539\_replaced([11159586](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25SGdPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11201126`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
(1.2) l2\_ps\_internal\_UlToDlIntraSchedUpdate

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11201133`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
Based on the checking result of activation algorithm, Pcell UL send result to Pcell DL.

If 3 continuous checking pass, Pcell UL will send l2\_ps\_internal\_UlToDlIntraSchedUpdate with SCellActivationCmdType = FR1\_UlDecision\_Activate\_Decision to Pcell DL.

If any checking is failed, Pcell UL will send l2\_ps\_internal\_UlToDlIntraSchedUpdate with SCellActivationCmdType = FR1\_UlDecision\_Deactivate\_Decision to Pcell DL. Pcell DL will save the flag to make final decision of activation.

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11201148`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11201153`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
(2.1) l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcellDpaMaxDaiInd

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11201159`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
Refer to 5G\_L2\_7287\_replaced([11158928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25N1BPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11201164`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
(2.2) PCsi transient handling

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11201177`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
PCsi transient phase is not available in joint DL/UL Scell activation because Scell can't schedule this UE until recieving FR1\_ACTIVATION\_ACK.

So here Scell only save PCsi with offset and period of PCell and all activated Scells.

[CB009169-AB] For FR1 T+F UL CA UE, no PCsi transient phase handling because no scheduling on FDD Scell overlapping slot and no PCsi carried on Scell PUSCH.  [End CB009169-AB]

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-8**  (ID: `11201184`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
(2.3) Inform SCell activation

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11201189`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
After the activation procedure finished in PCell and SCell (activation procedure including 1) MACCE for activation is ACKed, 2) activation timer up, 3) beam sync between PCell and SCell. All of these refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_290\_replaced([11195606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bfv2PfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SCell DL send l1\_ps\_internal\_DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with SCellActivationCmdType = FR1\_Activation\_ACK.

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-9**  (ID: `11201195`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
(2.4) Inform PCell UL and start buffer split

---

**8.3.2.1.1.0-2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11201202`)

Joint DL+UL SCell activation
After PCell DL receive l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_ScellUeScheulingResp, it sends  l2\_ps\_internal\_DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with SCellActivationCmdType = FR1\_Activation\_ACK to PCell UL to notify PCell UL can start buffer split, meanwhile PCell UL can stop the UE's activation checking.

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a process involving a UE (User Equipment), gNB\_DU (Next Generation NodeB - Distributed Unit), and PCELL/SCELL components. The diagram depicts the activation and deactivation of secondary cells (SCELLs) in relation to a primary cell (PCELL).
Here's a breakdown of the elements and their interactions:
**Components:**
\* **UE:** Represents the User Equipment.
\* **gNB\_DU:** Represents the Distributed Unit of the Next Generation NodeB.
\* **PCELL\_L2RT:** Primary Cell Layer 2 Receiver/Transmitter.
\* **PCELL\_DL:** Primary Cell Downlink.
\* **SCELL\_DLOnly\_L2RT:** Secondary Cell Downlink Only Layer 2 Receiver/Transmitter.
\* **SCELL1\_DL:** Secondary Cell 1 Downlink.
\* **SCELL\_JointDLUL\_L2RT:** Secondary Cell Joint Downlink/Uplink Layer 2 Receiver/Transmitter.
\* **SCELL2\_UL:** Secondary Cell 2 Uplink.
\* **PCELL and joint DL/UL SCELL in service:** A state indicating that the PCELL and joint DL/UL SCELL are in service.
\* **UE Inactive (SCell state in SCell):** A state indicating the UE is inactive and the SCELL is in a specific state.
**Sequence of Events:**
1. **1. DL Activation checking and Scell selection:**
\* This step involves checking DL activation and selecting an SCELL.
\* It's noted that "SCELL DLOnly is chosen".
\* Associated with this are two identifiers: `(5G_L1L2_FLOW_290)` and `(5G_UP_ALG_2724)`.
2. **2. Start transient phase:**
\* The diagram shows a transition into a transient phase.
\* **(2.1) l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd:** A message is sent from the gNB\_DU to the UE.
\* **Status:** `TRANSIENTSTART`
\* **Cause:** `ACTIVE`
\* **Content:** `SCELL DLOnly PCSI information`
\* **Save PCSI to remotePcell PCSI table, but not schedule pusch on these PCSI slots:** This is an internal action within the gNB\_DU, indicating that PCSI (Physical Cell Specific Information) is saved but PUSCH (Physical Uplink Shared Channel) is not scheduled on these slots yet.
\* **Ack for MACCE:** An acknowledgment for MACCE (Medium Access Control Control Element) is received.
\* **Activation timeout:** An activation timeout event occurs.
\* **(2.2) MACCE with activation:** MACCE is processed with activation.
3. **3. Stop transient phase:**
\* The diagram shows a transition out of the transient phase.
\* **(3.1) l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusind:** A message is sent from the gNB\_DU to the UE.
\* **Status:** `TRANSIENTSTOP`
\* **Cause:** `ACTIVE`
\* **Content:** `SCELL DL only PCSI information`
\* **Start scheduling on these PCSI slots:** An action indicating that scheduling on these PCSI slots will begin.
\* **(32) First beam sync and start scell scheduling (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_293):** This step involves first beam synchronization and starting SCELL scheduling.
\* **UE Active (SCell state in SCell):** The UE becomes active, and the SCELL is in an active state.
The diagram concludes with a URL at the bottom: `http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v8.3.7`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3394.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
 
link to "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1617\_Pcsi\_transient\_Act.signalling"

###### 8.3.2.1.2.0-2 Transient phase when DL only scell activation later Description (ID: 11201249)

**8.3.2.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201255`)

Transient phase when DL only scell activation later
1. DL Activation checking and Scell selection

---

**8.3.2.1.2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11201261`)

Transient phase when DL only scell activation later
Scell activation checking pass and Scell selection algorithm choose a DL only Scell. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2778\_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2716\_replaced([11121013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.1.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11201267`)

Transient phase when DL only scell activation later
2. Start transient phase

---

**8.3.2.1.2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201273`)

Transient phase when DL only scell activation later
(2.1) l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd

After Pcell decide to active this DL only Scell and before MACCE with activation send out, Pcell send l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd  to already in service joint DL/UL Scell to indicate the transient phase start.

The message with status = TRANSIENTSTART, cause = ACTIVE, content is PCSI information of this DL only Scell.

Joint DL/UL Scell save the content and status in local Pcsi table, do not schedule these slots with Pcsi of the DL only Scell.

(2.2) MACCE with activation

MACCE with activation bitmap send to UE and wait for ACK. It is legacy procedure of DL CA.

---

**8.3.2.1.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11201279`)

Transient phase when DL only scell activation later
3. Stop transient phase

---

**8.3.2.1.2.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11201286`)

Transient phase when DL only scell activation later
(3.1) l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd

After Pcell activation timer timeout, Pcell send l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd  to already in service joint DL/UL Scell to indicate the transient phase stop.

The message with status = TRANSIENTSTOP, cause = ACTIVE, content is PCSI information of this DL only Scell.

Joint DL/UL Scell start scheduling on these slots with Pcsi of the DL only Scell.

(3.2) First beam sync and start scell scheduling

Refer to DL 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_293\_replaced([11195644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfwdQPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a "SCell deactivation procedure" within a mobile network context, likely 5G. The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities, including "gNB\_DU", "PCELL", and "SCELL".
The diagram is divided into two main cases: "case1 Nomoral deactivation procedure" and "case2 Cancel deactivation procedure".
**Case 1: Nomoral deactivation procedure**
This case is further broken down into several steps:
\* **(1.1) Check if rrmBufferedDataTotal\_bytes = 0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2733)**: This is an initial check performed by the gNB\_DU.
\* **sCellDeactivationTimerGNB**: A timer related to SCell deactivation.
\* **(1.2) J2\_ps\_internal\_UITODIIntraSchedUpdate with FR1\_UIDecision\_Deactivate\_Decision**: An update message sent between entities.
\* **(2.1) Scell deactivation determination**: This step involves checking if "DL sCellDeactivationTimerGNB timeout" AND "UL SCellDeactivationTimerGNB timeout".
\* **(2.2) Deactivation sync between PCELL and SCELL**: This section details the synchronization of deactivation between the Primary Cell (PCELL) and Secondary Cell (SCELL).
\* `l2_ps_peerCtrl_SCellStatusInd` with `deactivateReq`
\* `l2_ps_peerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq` with `DEACTIVATE`
\* `l2_ps_internal_DIToUlIntraSchedUpdate` with `FR1_Deactivation_Decision`
\* `Clear harq`
\* `Clear PCSI of current Scell in PCSI table`
\* `l2_ps_peerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp` with `DEACTIVATE`
\* `l2_ps_internal_DIToUlIntraSchedUpdate` with `START_DEACTIVATION_TRANSIENT_PHASE_CMD`
\* **UE Inactive (SCell state in PCell)**: Indicates the state of the UE.
\* **(2.3) Send MACCE and stop buffer split**: This involves sending a MACCE message and stopping buffer splitting.
\* `l2_ps_internal_DIToUlIntraSchedUpdate` with `FR1_Deactivation_Decision`
\* **Stop buffer split procedure**: A sub-procedure.
\* `ref DL deactivation procedure (MACCE sending, stop PUCCH transient) 5G_L1L2_FLOW_293`: A reference to another procedure.
**Case 2: Cancel deactivation procedure**
This case handles the cancellation of the deactivation process.
\* **(3.1) Normal buffer split procedure**: This section deals with the normal buffer splitting.
\* `UL buffer split (5G_UP_ALG_9495)`: Indicates UL buffer splitting.
\* `l2_ps_peerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplitInd` with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes != 0`: An indication that buffer data is not zero.
\* **(3.2) Deactivation cancel**: This is the core of the cancellation procedure.
\* `l2_ps_internal_UITODIIntraSchedUpdate` with `FR1_UIDecision_Deactivate_Cancel`: A message to cancel deactivation.
\* **Check if rrmBufferedDataTotal\_bytes = 0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5733)**: A check performed during cancellation.
The diagram also shows a general state of "PCELL and SCELL in service" and "UE Active (SCell state in PCell)" at the beginning, and "UE Inactive (SCell state in PCell)" during the deactivation process.
The bottom of the image contains a URL: `http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v6.3.7`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3405.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
file: "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1749\_BuffBased\_Deact.signalling"

---

###### 8.3.2.1.3.0-2 Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation Description (ID: 11201320)

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201325`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
1.UL Scell buffer based deactivation

---

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11201332`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2733\_replaced([11121319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqX7c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

(1.1) Check if rrmBufferedDataTotal\_bytes

Scell UL will always check if rrmBufferedDataTotal\_bytes = 0 in case there is an update of rrmBufferedDataTotal\_bytes, two scenarios is taken into account: UL scheduling or receive buffer split from Pcell.

If yes, start UL sCellDeactivationTimerGNB.

(1.2) l2\_ps\_internal\_UlToDlIntraSchedUpdate

After UL sCellDeactivationTimerGNB timeout, Scell UL send l2\_ps\_internal\_UlToDlIntraSchedUpdate with FR1\_UlDecision\_Deactivate\_Decision to notify Scell DL.

Scell DL won't trigger Scell deactivation procedure until DL sCellDeactivationTimerGNB timeout as well.

---

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11201339`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
(2.1) Scell deactivation determination

---

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201345`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
Note: (2.1) (2.2) (2.3) descripe case1 normal deactivation procedure

If DL sCellDeactivationTimerGNB and UL sCellDeactivationTimerGNB both timeout, SCell DL start deactivation sync between PCell and SCell including l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_SCellStatusInd with deactivationReq, l2\_ps\_ctrl\_SCellUeSchedulingReq with deactivation and corresponding l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_SCellUeSchedulingResp, which is legacy procedure introduced by DL CA by 1390-D.

Only DL timeout or only UL timeout won't trigger Scell deactivation.

---

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11201351`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
(2.2) Deactivation sync between PCell and SCell

---

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11201357`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
Deactivation procedure is legacy procedure refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_311\_replaced([11195870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfxrYfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

New part introduced by UL CA is that when SCell DL receive l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_SCellUeSchedulingReq, SCell DL sends l2\_ps\_internal\_DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with FR1\_Deactivation\_Decision to SCell UL, SCell UL clear UL harq and clear PCSI of current SCell in PCSI table.

---

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11201364`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
(2.3) Send MACCE for deactivation and stop buffer split

---

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11201369`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
After PCell DL receive l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_SCellUeSchedulingResp, it sends l2\_ps\_internal\_DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with FR1\_Deactivation\_Decision to PCell UL and then buffer split will be stopped.

---

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11201374`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
(3.1)  SCell deactivation cancel due to valid buffer split

---

**8.3.2.1.3.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11201380`)

Joint DL+UL SCell deactivation
Note: (3.1) (3.2) descripe case 2 cancel deactivation procedure

SCell deactivation may be cancelled if PCell UL send valid buffer split with valid buffer size by sending l2\_ps\_internal\_DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with FR1\_UlDecision\_Deactivate\_Cancel.

This action is taken before SCell DL don't make the decision of deactivation yet.

[Before CB009169-AB] This case is applied when DL only Scell deactivation before UL Scell still in actived
 
[CB009169-AB] This case is only applied for FR1 F+T UL CA UE when DL only Scell deactivation with a UL Scell still in actived
 
For FR1 T+F UL CA UE, no PCsi transient phase handling (i.e. l1\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd relavant handling) because no scheduling on FDD Scell overlapping slot and no PCsi carried on Scell PUSCH. 
Other deactivation procedure is normal.
[End CB009169-AB]
 
 
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a deactivation procedure for a Secondary Cell (SCell) in a 5G network. The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities, including the gNB\_DU (gNB Distributed Unit), PCell (Primary Cell), and UE (User Equipment).
The diagram is structured into several phases:
1. **Deactivation trigger**: The process begins with a deactivation trigger, followed by a decision for the SCell to be deactivated. An `ScellStatusInd` message with `DEACTIVATEREQ` is sent.
2. **Start transient phase**: This phase involves the `l2_ps_peerCtrl_PcsiStatusInd` message being sent with `Status: TRANSIENTSTART`, `Cause: DEACTIVE`, and `Content: SCELL DLOnly PCSI information`. A note indicates to "Stop scheduling on these Pcsi slots".
3. **DI deactivation procedure**: This step involves MACCE sending and stopping PUCCH transient, identified by the flow `(5G_L1L2_FLOW_314)`.
4. **Stop transient phase**: This phase involves another `l2_ps_peerCtrl_PcsiStatusInd` message, this time with `Status: TRANSIENTSTOP`, `Cause: DEACTIVE`, and `Content: SCELL DL only PCSI information`. A note indicates to "remove deactived scell pcsi in pcsi table".
The diagram also shows the UE state changing from "UE Active (SCell state in SCell)" to "UE Inactive (SCell state in SCell)".
The top section of the diagram outlines the different L2RT (Layer 2 Relay) entities involved: PCell\_L2RT (with PCell\_UL and PCell\_DL), SCELL\_DLOnly\_L2RT, and SCELL\_JointDLUL\_L2RT (with SCELL2\_UL). It also indicates that the PCell and joint DL/UL SCELL are in service.
The bottom right corner contains a URL: `http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v8.3.7`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3421.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
link to "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1623\_Pcsi\_transient\_Deact.signalling"

Transient phase when DL only scell deactivation
1. Deactivation trigger

---

**8.3.2.1.4.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11201441`)

Transient phase when DL only scell deactivation
Scell deactivation triggered by Scell itself and Scell send ScellStatusInd with DEACTIVATEREQ to Pcell, refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_331\_replaced([11196055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfySe_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.1.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11201447`)

Transient phase when DL only scell deactivation
2. Start transient phase

---

**8.3.2.1.4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201454`)

Transient phase when DL only scell deactivation
(2.1) l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd

When PCell receive ScellSchedulingInd with DEACTIVATEREQ, it send l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd to already in service joint DL/UL Scell to indicate the transient phase start.

The message with status = TRANSIENTSTART, cause = DEACTIVE, content is PCSI information of this DL only Scell.

Joint DL/UL Scell stop scheduling pusch on these slots with Pcsi of the DL only Scell.

---

**8.3.2.1.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11201459`)

Transient phase when DL only scell deactivation
3.Deactivation procedure

---

**8.3.2.1.4.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11201466`)

Transient phase when DL only scell deactivation
Scell deactivation is legacy procedure in DL CA, refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_313\_replaced([11195882](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfxrY_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.1.4.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11201472`)

Transient phase when DL only scell deactivation
4. Stop transient phase

---

**8.3.2.1.4.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11201479`)

Transient phase when DL only scell deactivation
(4.1) l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd

After Pcell pucch transient timer timeout, it means deactivation procedure almost finished, gNB and UE sync finished. So Pcell send l2\_ps\_peerCtrl\_PcsiStatusInd to joint DL/UL Scell to indicate the transient phase stop.

The message with status = TRANSIENTSTOP, cause = DEACTIVE, content is PCSI information of this DL only Scell.

Joint DL/UL Scell remove these Pcsi information from local Pcsi table.

(4.2) stop PUCCH transient

Refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_313\_replaced([11195882](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfxrY_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating communication protocols between different network entities in a 5G system. The entities involved are 5G\_UE, PCell\_5G\_L1\_UL, PCell\_5G\_L1\_DL, PCell\_LO, PCell\_5G\_L2PS, gNB\_DU, SCell\_5G\_L1\_UL, SCell\_5G\_L1\_DL, SCell\_LO, SCell\_5G\_L2PS, and SCell\_L2RT.
The diagram depicts two main scenarios: PCell UL scheduling and SCell scheduling.
**PCell UL Scheduling:**
This section details the process of the PCell handling UL scheduling. It starts with the 5G\_UE sending a PDCCH signal (2.2) to the PCell. The PCell then sends a `DIData_PdcchSendReq(DCI)` (2.1) to the gNB\_DU. The diagram shows a conditional block (2.3) indicating that if PCell UL scheduling occurs on an overlapping slot, a `PsPeerCtrl_PcellUISchedulingind` (2.4) is sent. The PCell receives a `UIData_PuschReceiveReq` (2.5) from the 5G\_UE, followed by a PUSCH transmission (2.6). The PCell then sends back `UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU` (2.7), `UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD` (2.8), `PuschReceiveRespPs` (2.9), and `PuschReceiveRespLo` (2.10) to the 5G\_UE. Finally, a `LoCtrl_UIMacPduReceivelnd` (2.11) is sent to the gNB\_DU.
There's a sub-scenario within PCell UL scheduling where the PCell checks if it needs to receive PUCCH. If so, it receives a `UIData_PucchReceiveReq` (2.12) from the 5G\_UE, followed by PUCCH transmission (2.13). The PCell then responds with `UIData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD` (2.14) and `UIData_PucchReceiveRespPs` (2.15).
**SCell Scheduling:**
This section illustrates the SCell's role in scheduling. It begins with the gNB\_DU sending a `DIData_PdcchSendReq(DCI)` (3.1) to the SCell. Similar to the PCell scenario, there's a conditional block (3.3) for SCell UL scheduling on an overlapping slot, which triggers `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUISchedulingind` (3.3) and `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUIHousekeepingReportind` (3.4). The SCell receives a `UIData_PuschReceiveReq` (3.5) from the 5G\_UE, followed by PUSCH transmission (3.6). The SCell then sends back `UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU` (3.7) and `PuschReceiveRespPs` (3.8).
There's a conditional block indicating "if CSlover Scell PUSCH for UL CAUE". Another conditional block states "if there is UCI over Scell PUSCH, forward to Pcell". This leads to `UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD` (3.9) being sent, followed by `PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschHarqD` (3.10) and `PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschPs` (3.11). A note indicates that the PCell handles UCI and forwards it to SCells, reusing UCI over PCell PUSCH (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_450).
Finally, there's a conditional block for "MAC-CE over Scell PUSCH or DRB over transmission", which results in `PuschReceiveRespLo` (3.13) and `LoCtrl_UIMacPduReceiveInd` (3.14) being sent. The diagram concludes with `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlInfoUpdateind` (3.15).
The diagram also includes activation boxes for DL-UL SCell, indicating that it is activated and in a specific state within PCell and SCell. There are also references to specific flow identifiers like `5G_L1_IF_70`, `5G_L1_IF_183`, `5G_L2_IF_875`, `5G_L1L2_FLOW_1220`, `5G_L2_694`, `5G_L2_IF_2210`, `5G_L1_IF_212`, and `5G_L1L2_FLOW_450`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3434.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

For UL Scell scheduling with DCI0\_1, the Fake Dai is applied same with Pcell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4466\_replaced([11178897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB009169-AB] Note: it's not applied to FR1 TDD + FDD UL CA refer to 5G\_L2\_7108\_replaced([11160809](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25W-_fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  [End CB009169-AB]

**8.3.2.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11201538`)

---

**8.3.2.2.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11201551`)

UL CA HARQ for inter-L2RT
The relationship for below 3 messages need Sync between Pcell and Scell:

Step(2.5): PUSCH in PCell, represent there is UL schedued in Pcell;

Step(3.5): PUSCH in SCell,represent there is UL schedued in Scell;

Step(2.12): PUCCH in PCell, means no any PUSCH present, AN or CSI will be present in PUCCH if have;

The possible CSI and HARQ bits for DL which over on PUCCH/PUSCH obey the rule as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3609\_replaced([11159986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If there is any PUSCH in Pcell or Scell for UE happen on the Ul slot, then PUCCH in Pcell is not needed.

step(2.5) and Step(2.12) are both on the PCell, so the whether PUCCH in Pcell should be present or not depending on intra sync from SCell scheduling report by PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUlSchedulingInd in Step(3.3).

In FR1 UL CA SW deployment,Pcell and Scell on different L2-PS, the sync message maybe delayed:

When there is no Step(2.5), and Step(3.3) is later than the PUCCH sending time from PCell to L1, PCell should blindly try PUCCH receiving with harqProcessIndex = 100 as 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In this case, for the harqProcessIndex = 100 message, when PCell receives its PUCCH receiving response(Step2.14/Step2.15) from L1, if PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUlSchedulingInd has already arrived in PCell for sure, they should be ignored(Since no PUCCH sending by UE actually).

[CB009169-AB] Note: Step(2.3), Step(2.4) and the harqProcessIndex = 100 process is not applied to FR1 TDD + FDD UL CA refer to 5G\_L2\_7108\_replaced([11160809](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25W-_fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  [End CB009169-AB]

---

**8.3.2.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11201557`)

UL CA HARQ for inter-L2RT
(3) Scell UL Scheduling and HARQ\_D and CSI on SCell PUSCH

---

**8.3.2.2.0-2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11201576`)

UL CA HARQ for inter-L2RT
Scell UL PDCCH/PUSCH scheduling, refer to 5G\_L2\_7618\_replaced([11160929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25YNEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

According 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3609\_replaced([11159986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), on overlapping UL slots, only if no explicit uplink grant (DCI) on PCell, possible HARQ feedback for DL and CSI are multiplexed on SCell PUSCH if SCell UL scheduling happens.

Step2.4

[Before CB006449-AA]

For all cases apart from UL CA 2CC F+F and PCell on ABIL:

PCell sends PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlSchedulingInd to SCell with whether there is PUSCH in PCell and the detailed number of HARQ\_D bits (only PCell knows total DL CA AN bits) as 5G\_L2\_IF\_2130\_replaced([10980097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VfmTvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For UL CA 2CC F+F and PCell on ABIL:

PCell DL Scheduler sends PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlSchedulingInd to SCell with pCellUlSchedulingIndType set to DlHarqBitsOnly and number of HARQ\_D bits (UL Grant information is omitted). If there is no UE with number of DL HARQ A/N bits grater than zero (UEs awaiting DL transmition confirmation), then message is not sent.

PCell UL Scheduler sends PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlSchedulingInd to SCell with pCellUlSchedulingIndType set to UlGrantOnly and whether there is PUSCH in PCell (number of DL HARQ A/N bits is omitted). If there are no UL Grants to be indicated message is not sent.

[CB006449-AA]

For UL CA 2CC (F+F and PCell on ABIL) or (T+T):

PCell DL Scheduler sends PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlSchedulingInd to SCell with pCellUlSchedulingIndType set to DlHarqBitsOnly and number of HARQ\_D bits (UL Grant information is omitted). If there is no UE with number of DL HARQ A/N bits grater than zero (UEs awaiting DL transmition confirmation), then message is not sent.

PCell UL Scheduler sends PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlSchedulingInd to SCell with pCellUlSchedulingIndType set to UlGrantOnly and whether there is PUSCH in PCell (number of DL HARQ A/N bits is omitted). If there are no UL Grants to be indicated message is not sent.

For all other cases of UL CA:

PCell sends PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlSchedulingInd to SCell with whether there is PUSCH in PCell and the detailed number of HARQ\_D bits (only PCell knows total DL CA AN bits) as 5G\_L2\_IF\_2130\_replaced([10980097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VfmTvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB006449-AA]

SCell decided AN bits or CSI over Scell PUSCH as 5G\_L2\_7618\_replaced([11160929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25YNEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) based on information in  PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlSchedulingInd.

If there is any HARQ\_D bit or CSI bit multiplexed on SCell PUSCH, SCell should forward the HARQ\_D and CSI decoded from L1 to PCell by Step 3.10, Step3.11 when SCell receive 3.8, 3.9.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "UL TA Sync (Inter L2-RT UL CA)" process. The diagram depicts interactions between different components within a gNB\_DU (gNB Distributed Unit).
The gNB\_DU is divided into two main parts: "Primary L2RT" and "Secondary L2RT". Each of these parts further comprises two components:
- **Primary L2RT**: "PCell 5G-L2PS" and "PCell 5G-L2LO"
- **Secondary L2RT**: "SCell 5G-L2PS" and "SCell 5G-L2LO"
The diagram shows a series of numbered steps representing messages or actions exchanged between these components:
1. **(1) TA sync triggering**: An initial event that triggers the synchronization process.
2. **(2) postpone TAC timer**: An action to postpone a timer related to TAC (Timing Advance Command).
3. **(3) PsPeerCtrl\_PcellTaSync**: A message sent from "PCell 5G-L2LO" to "PCell 5G-L2PS".
4. **(4) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellTaReport**: A message sent from "PCell 5G-L2PS" to "SCell 5G-L2PS".
5. **(5) compute TAC**: An action to compute the TAC.
6. **Opt**: This label indicates an optional step.
7. **(6) send TAC**: An action to send the computed TAC.
8. **(7) reset long term TO**: An action to reset a long-term timeout.
9. **(8) PsPeerCtrl\_PcellTaSync**: Another message sent from "PCell 5G-L2LO" to "PCell 5G-L2PS".
10. **(9) reset long term TO**: Another action to reset a long-term timeout.
The diagram uses vertical lines to represent the lifelines of each component and horizontal arrows to show the direction of messages or actions. The "Opt" label suggests that steps 6, 7, 8, and 9 are part of an optional flow within the overall process.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3448.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

#### 8.3.2.3.0-2 UL Timing Advance Sync Description: (ID: 11201607)

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201611`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
(1) TA sync triggering

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11201618`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
When PCell detects expiry of a timer with a period length of rdTacPeriodicity\_ms(refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3303\_replaced([11150011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksRY6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or on demand TA update is needed(refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10031\_replaced([11150239](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksSnCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a CA UE with activated SCell with UL configured, the activation status defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2804\_replaced([11121880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), TA sync between PCell and Scell is triggered.

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11201624`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
(2) postpone TAC timer

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11201636`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
For the UL CA UE, PCell postpone this UE’s TA timer for [Before CB009169-AB] 2 PCell slots [CB009169-AB] 3 milliseconds [End CB009169-AB], to wait for the SCell long term timing offset response. If PCell does not receive SCell long term timing offset response within [Before CB009169-AB] 2 slots [CB009169-AB] 3 milliseconds [End CB009169-AB], the SCell response is considered as timeout and SCell' timing offset weight is set to 0, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3316\_replaced([11150211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksSnB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [CB009169-AB] Once PCell received PsPeerCtrl\_ScellTaReport from SCell within the 3 milliseconds postponed timing, PCell will reset TA timer expiry time to next slot to unblock TAC calculation and send process.  [End CB009169-AB]

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11201642`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
(3) PCell send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellTaSync(action=taQuery) to SCell

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11201648`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
PCell filter out all UL CA UEs that need to be queried on one single slot, construct message PsPeerCtrl\_PcellTaSync with action=taQuery as per 5G\_L2\_IF\_2429\_replaced([10980678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VkexPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and send this message to SCell 5G-L2-PS which is activated and with UL configured to query long term timing offset computation result from on SCell.

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11201653`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
(4) SCell send PsPeerCtrl\_ScellTaReport to PCell

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13487597`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
After SCell received query request from PCell, Scell construct PsPeerCtrl\_ScellTaReport as per 5G\_L2\_IF\_2446\_replaced([10980720](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vkezfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and respond this message to PCell. PsPeerCtrl\_ScellTaReport includes [Before CB015279-F] uePuschLongTermTimingOffsetSCell and puschWeightSCell [CB015279-F] rrmUePuschLongTermOffsetPower, puschWeight, rrmUeSrsLongTermOffsetPower and srsWeight [End CB015279-F] of UL CA UEs that PCell queried.

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11201665`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
(5) PCell compute combined long term timing offset

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13487613`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
After the postponed TAC timer in step (2) is expired, PCell collect UL CA UEs’ [Before CB015279-F] uePuschLongTermTimingOffsetSCell and puschWeightSCell from SCell, and compute combined long term timing offsetCompute algorithm as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3315\_replaced([11150206](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksSnBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [CB015279-F] long term timing offsets and weights (PUSCH and SRS based). Dependent on TAG of Scell combined or separate algorithm is used to compute TAC, for details see: [11150206](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksSnBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). [End CB015279-F].

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11201676`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
(6-7) PCell send TAC if checking actions are passed and reset long term timing offset

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11201682`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
This part has not changed, detailed information refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3303\_replaced([11150011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksRY6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11201687`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
(8) PCell send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellTaSync(action=taReset) to SCell

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11201694`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
PCell filter out all CA UEs that need to be reset on one single slot, construct message PsPeerCtrl\_PcellTaSync with action= taReset as per 5G\_L2\_IF\_2429\_replaced([10980678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VkexPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and send this message to SCell 5G-L2-PS which is activated and with UL configured.

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-8**  (ID: `11201699`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
(9) SCell reset long term timing offset

---

**8.3.2.3.0-2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11201704`)

UL Timing Advance Sync
After SCell received reset request from PCell, SCell reset long term timing offset of itself. This reset action has not changed, detailed information refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3303\_replaced([11150011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksRY6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\* **case3: BSR from SCell**: Includes `LoCtrl_UIMacPduReceiveInd`, `Scell check BSR and over transmissionm, forward to Pcell`, `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlInfoUpdateInd`, and `Pcell update housekeeping`.
\* **case4: data unbalance after PCell scheduling**: References `Pcell UL scheduling, refer to 5G_L1L2_FLOW_1491` and `Pcell update housekeeping`.
\* **case5: data unbalance check after Scell scheduling report**: Contains `SCell scheduling newTx with Data`, `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUIHousekeepingReportInd`, and `Pcell update housekeeping`.
\* **opt (6.1) buffer split condition reached**: This is an optional path that includes `PsPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplitInd` and `Scell update housekeeping`.
\* **opt some CA UE's buffer split state changes**: Another optional path with `LoCtrl_UIBuffer Split Statusind` and `LoData_UeDataDelivery StatusInd`.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "UL Buffer Split For Inter-L2PS UL CA" process. The diagram depicts interactions between different components: PCell\_LO, PCell\_L2RT, PCell\_5G\_L2PS, SCell\_L2RT, SCell\_5G\_L2PS, SCell\_LO, and L2\_HI, all within the gNB\_DU.
The diagram is structured into several cases, each representing a specific scenario or condition:
\* **case1: UL Scell active**: This case shows the activation of UL Scell.
\* **case2: BSR from PCell**: This case details the process of receiving a Buffer Status Report (BSR) from PCell.
\* **case3: BSR from SCell**: This case describes the handling of a BSR received from SCell, including checks and forwarding to PCell.
\* **case4: data unbalance after PCell scheduling**: This case covers scenarios where data imbalance occurs after PCell scheduling. It includes a reference to "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1491" and conditional updates based on the number of CC NFDs.
\* **case5: data unbalance check after Scell scheduling report**: This case deals with data imbalance checks after receiving a scheduling report from SCell. It also includes conditional updates based on CC NFDs.
\* **case7: PCell NFD state change**: This case illustrates changes in PCell's NFD (Network Functionality Discovery) state, including entering or exiting NFD and checking data unbalance.
\* **case8: SCell NFD state change**: This case shows SCell's NFD state changes, including receiving information updates and PCell recording SCell's NFD state.
\* **opt (6.1) buffer split condition reached**: This optional case is triggered when the buffer split condition is met. It involves a buffer split indication and Scell update housekeeping.
\* **opt some CA UE's buffer split state changes**: This optional case handles changes in buffer split states for some CA (Carrier Aggregation) UEs, involving status registration and data delivery status indication.
The diagram uses various message types, including asynchronous messages (indicated by arrows), conditional branches (alt), and optional steps (opt). The components are arranged vertically, representing their lifelines, and messages are shown as horizontal arrows between these lifelines. The background colors highlight different sections or cases within the diagram.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3474.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

#### 8.3.2.4.0-2 UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling Description: (ID: 11201778)

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201784`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
case1, case 2, case3, case4, case5, case7, case8 Buffer Split trigger

---

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11201794`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10281\_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for buffer split trigger:

case1: UL scell activatioin  --> Trigger-2 defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10281\_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

case2/case3: BSR from Pcell or Scell --> Trigger-1 defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10281\_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before CB006137-C]

case4/5: BSR split between PCell and SCell is not match. Unbalanced check based on Pcell or Scell UL scheduling --> Trigger-3 defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10281\_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB006137-C]

case4/5: BSR split between PCell and SCell is not match. Unbalanced check based on Pcell or Scell UL scheduling --> Trigger-3 defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10281\_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when UE is not under one CC NFD state, and  unbalanced check based on Pcell or Scell UL scheduling --> Trigger-7 defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10281\_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when UE is not under one CC NFD state.

case7: If PCell enter/exit NFD lead UE into one CC NFD state, then check if the trigger as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14522\_replaced([11122787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is fulfilled.

case8: If PCell received SCell event of enter/exit NFD, then UE is led into one CC NFD state, PCell check if the trigger as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14522\_replaced([11122787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is fulfilled.

[End CB006137-C]

---

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11201800`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
(3.1) Check BSR and data over transmission

---

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201806`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
If there is up to date BSR decoded from SCell LoCtrl\_UlMacPduReceiveInd, SCell should transfer the BSR to PCell to update UL buffer and may trigger buffer split as  5G\_L2\_7624\_replaced([11160998](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25YNHvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

On receiving SCell LoCtrl\_UlMacPduReceiveInd, SCell also check if data over transmission as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9787\_replaced([11203724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwg_sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If there is any data transmission on SCell, report it to PCell via PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUlInfoUpdateInd. SCell check for data over transmission and PCell process should be as 5G\_L2\_7630\_replaced([11161327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25apU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11201810`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
(2.2)(3.2)(4.2)(4.3)(5.3)(5.4)(6.3)PCell/SCell update housekeeping

---

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11201822`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
PCell and SCell shall do housekeeping as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5114\_replaced([11203638](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfxnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and apply the buffer split logic as 5G\_L2\_7630\_replaced([11161327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25apU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Whether PCell receive BSR from PCell\_LO or receive BSR forwarded by SCell, PCell should do housekeeping (2.2), (3.2) to update UE's buffer as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5128\_replaced([11203789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwg_vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),  and applicate the buffer split logic as 5G\_L2\_7565\_replaced([11146575](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Gat_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_7630\_replaced([11161327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25apU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

After PCell newTx UL scheduling, PCell should update huosekeeping(4.2) [CB006137-C] or (4.3) [End CB006137-C] as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5124\_replaced([11203753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwg_t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). After SCell newTx Scheduling, SCell should report (5.2) [CB006137-C] or (5.4) [End CB006137-C] to PCell and PCell do housekeeping as 5G\_L2\_7613\_replaced([11146456](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24FzpfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_7630\_replaced([11161327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25apU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

After every buffer split in PCell arrives in SCell via (6.2), SCell should do housekeeping(6.3) as 5G\_L2\_7607\_replaced([11146405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24FMnfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and  5G\_L2\_7630\_replaced([11161327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25apU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11201827`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
(5.1) SCell Scheduling newTx

---

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11201833`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
SCell can schedule newTx with none zero data volume split from PCell.

For every newTx scheduling, calculate eTh as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9492\_replaced([11204535](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); do housekeeping as 5G\_L2\_7630\_replaced([11161327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25apU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

After every newTx scheduling, SCell send PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUlHousekeepingReportInd to PCell.

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
(6.1)Check Buffer Split Condition

---

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11201852`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
[CB006137-C] If UE is not under one CC NFD state, [End CB006137-C] Buffer split condition should be checked as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9496\_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9591\_replaced([11122888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqhFYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and L2 entity detail for buffer split is as 5G\_L2\_7624\_replaced([11160998](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25YNHvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

when buffer split algorithm done, Pcell send split buffer message 6.2 to Scell.

Scell update housekeeping as 5G\_L2\_7630\_replaced([11161327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25apU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and  make UL scheduling based on latest splited buffer.

[CB006137-C] If UE is under one CC NFD state, no buffer split condition should be checked or be updated. [End CB006137-C]

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11201860`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
(6.4) (6.5) Check CA UEs' buffer split state

---

**8.3.2.4.0-2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11201872`)

UL CA Buffer Split for FR1 CA Scheduling
If some CA UE's buffer split state change, the indication shall be sent from Scell L2-PS to Scell L2-LO with a mssage [Before CNI-122708]LoCtrl\_UlBufferSplitStatusInd[CNI-122708]LoCtrl\_UlBufferSplitStatusReq[End CNI-122708] (5G\_L2\_IF\_2833\_replaced([10985232](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WGDPPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Status change means UL buffer split size on SCell change from zero to non zero, or from non zero to zero. If only some CA UE's buffer size changed from a non zero value to another non zero vlaue, a message [Before CNI-122708]LoCtrl\_UlBufferSplitStatusInd[CNI-122708]LoCtrl\_UlBufferSplitStatusReq[End CNI-122708] is not needed to be sent.

After receiving [Before CNI-122708]LoCtrl\_UlBufferSplitStatusInd[CNI-122708]LoCtrl\_UlBufferSplitStatusReq[End CNI-122708], L2-LO will fill the CA UE' buffer split state in ulBufferSplitStatus for LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_946\_replaced([10986019](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WMJ1vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If any CA UE's ulBufferSplitStatus changes, a message LoData\_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd need be sent to L2-HI, and that is triggered by legacy period sending framework but not sent immediately (refer to 5G\_L2\_1931\_replaced([11217086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_CJKfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For the details how L2-HI use CA UEs' buffer split state, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10516\_replaced([11122476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1919\_splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep Calculation During State Change For Inter-L2PS UL CA:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep Calculation For Different cases" within a gNB\_DU (Next Generation NodeB - Distributed Unit). The diagram depicts interactions between different components: PCell\_LO\_UL, PCell\_L2RT, PCell\_PS\_UL, SCell\_L2RT, SCell\_PS\_UL, and SCell\_LO\_UL.
The diagram is divided into three main cases, indicated by "alt" blocks:
**Case 1: OverPower State Change Trigger**
\* A trigger occurs for an "overPower State Change".
\* The state transitions from "non overpower to overpower".
**Case 2: PHR from Pcell during OverPower Trigger**
\* This case is triggered by a "PHR from Pcell druing over Power trigger".
\* (2.1) `LoCtrl_UIMacPduReceiveInd` is received from L2-LO, containing PHR information from both Pcell and Scell.
\* (2.2) A check is performed to see if the CA UE (Carrier Aggregation User Equipment) is in an overpower state.
**Case 3: PHR from Scell during OverPower Trigger**
\* This case is triggered by a "PHR from Scell druing over Power trigger".
\* (3.1) `LoCtrl_UIMacPduReceiveInd` is received from L2-LO, containing PHR information from both Pcell and Scell.
\* (3.2) `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlInfoUpdateInd` is sent, including Pcell's PHR.
\* (3.3) A check is performed to see if the CA UE is in an overpower state.
Following these initial cases, a common set of steps occurs:
\* (4) `PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlPhrForwardInd` is sent, including an `efficiencyRequest` and Scell's PHR, depending on the specific case.
\* (5) `Calculate efficiencyPerPRB` is performed.
\* (6) `PsPeerCtrl_ScellEfficiencyReportInd` is sent with the calculated `efficiencyPerPrb`.
\* (7) `Calculate efficiencyPerPRB` is performed again.
\* (8) `Calculate splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep` is performed.
\* (9) `PsPeerCtrl_PcellPowerControlInd` is sent with both Pcell and Scell power adjustment steps.
The diagram also includes a footer with the text "http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v8.3.7".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3498.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1919\_splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep Calculation For Difference Cases  For Inter-L2PS UL CA.signalling" file in

---

##### 8.3.2.5.1.0-2 efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation Description: (ID: 11201923)

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201929`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep Calculation Trigger for Different Cases

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11201934`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
Trigger conditions to splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation are described in 5G\_L2\_8698\_replaced([11161699](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25b3dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1941\_replaced([11201907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgVFAPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) desribe the porcess for different cases. Case 1 describes changing from non overpower to overpower state, case2 and case3 describes receiving (v)PHR from Pcell or Scell if CA UE is in overpower state seperately. In summary, splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep will be cacluated on Pcell when receiving PsPeerCtrl\_ScellEfficiencyReportInd from Scell.

Notes:

1. efficiencyPerPRB is calculated on both Pcell and Scell. The time when to calculate depend on different scenarios, refer to 5G\_L2\_8663\_replaced([11161689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25b3dPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detail. Scell's efficiencyPerPRB should be forwarded to Pcell.
2. splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep is calculated only on Pcell side. After receiving Scell's efficiencyPerPRB, splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calcualtion will start, and calculation result will be sent to Scell.
3. To make process common, a measge PsPeerCtrl\_ScellEfficiencyReportInd is also sent for case 3.
4. Only a single should be sent if CA UE's state is changed to overpower and PHR are triggered in the same slot.

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11201942`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
(1.1) Non overpower to overpower Change

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11201949`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
If UL CA UE's overpower state changes from non overpower to overpower, efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep need to be calculated.

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11201955`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
(2.1) (3.1) (3.2) Multi PHR from Pcell or Scell

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11201967`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
(2.2) (3.3)  Overpower State Check

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11201974`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
After UL CA is activated, multi PHR information including Pcell and Scell(s) will report from CA UE. Multi PHR will be received by a single serving cell, the receiving serving cell will store its own PHR information, and forward PHR that is not its own to peer serving cell(s). Refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1570\_replaced([11202890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgaklPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for forward procedure.

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11201980`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
(4) with efficiencyRequest or (v)PHR Fowarded from Pcell

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11201985`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
If multi (v)PHR is received on Pcell, Pcell should send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlPhrForwardIndnd (refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_2682\_replaced([10980279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vhbc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to Scell.

For different cases described in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1918\_replaced([11201901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgUeCPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), different IEs in PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlPhrForwardInd should be filled as follow.

1. efficiencyRequest is present but uePhrForwardInfo not present for case 1 and case 3.
2. Both uePhrForwardInfo and efficiencyRequest are present for case 2.

For efficiencyPerPRB calculation description, refer to 5G\_L2\_8663\_replaced([11161689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25b3dPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11201991`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
(5) (6) Calculate efficiencyPerPRB on Scell

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11201996`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
After receiving  PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlPhrForwardIndnd (refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_2682\_replaced([10980279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vhbc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with efficiencyRequest, Scell should calculate UEs’ efficiencyPerPrb. CA UEs' efficiencyPerPrb value on Scell should be sent in PsPeerCtrl\_ScellEfficiencyReportInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_2933\_replaced([10980962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vm7APu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after calculation finish.

For efficiencyPerPRB calculation description, refer to 5G\_L2\_8663\_replaced([11161689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25b3dPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11202002`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
(7) (8) (9) Calculate efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep on Pcell

---

**8.3.2.5.1.0-2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11202008`)

efficiencyPerPRB and splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation
After receiving PsPeerCtrl\_ScellEfficiencyReportInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_2933\_replaced([10980962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vm7APu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), Pcell should calculate UEs’ efficiencyPerPRB using its own PHR information. After both Pcell's and Scell's efficiencyRequest, Pcell will start calculating splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep. After splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation is finished, Pcell will send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellPowerControlInd with both Pcell’s and Scell’s splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep to Scell.

For splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep calculation, refer to 5G\_L2\_8698\_replaced([11161699](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25b3dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1812\_UL Initial Split TxPower For Inter-L2PS UL CA:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating different cases of cell activation and resume triggers in a gNB\_DU (next-generation NodeB - Distributed Unit). The diagram shows interactions between PCell (Primary Cell) and SCell (Secondary Cell) components, specifically their DL (Downlink) and UL (Uplink) interfaces, as well as L2RT (Layer 2 Relay) and management interfaces.
The diagram is divided into five distinct cases:
**Case 1: UL scell activation trigger**
\* `SCellActivationManagerInd` is triggered with `FR1_Activation_ACK`.
\* This leads to `trigger2 of buffer Split success(5G_UP_ALG_10281)`.
\* Subsequently, `psPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplit` is called with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes !=0` and `scell initialSplitTxPower`.
\* Finally, `Scell start UL schedluing` is initiated with `scell splitTxPower = scell initial SplitTxPower`.
**Case 2: bufferSplit stop or scell(with only overlap slot) resume trigger**
\* `rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower` times out (when `scell` with only overlap slot is suspended) and `bufferSplit` is triggered by BSR success.
\* `psPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplit` is called with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes !=0` and `scell initialSplitTxPower`.
\* `Scell start UL schedluing` is initiated with `scell splitTxPower = scell initial SplitTxPower`.
**Case 3: scell(with non-overlap slot) resume trigger**
\* `scell(with non-overlap slot) resume success(5G_UP_ALG_10923)` occurs, and `bufferSplit` is triggered by BSR success. (No need to start `rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower`).
\* `psPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplit` is called with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes !=0` and `scell initialSplitTxPower`.
\* `Scell start UL schedluing` is initiated with `scell splitTxPower = scell initial SplitTxPower`.
**Case 4: pcell resume trigger**
\* `pcell resume success(5G_UP_ALG_10923)` is received.
\* `psPeerCtrl_ScellUIControlInd` is called with `powerResume, initialSplitTxPower`.
\* `Pcell start UL schedluing` is initiated in an overlap slot with `pcell splitTxPower = pcell initialSplitTxPower`.
**Case 5: joint DL&UL Scell overheating resume**
\* This case refers to `5G_L1L2_FLOW_2077`.
\* `PCell Ul receives overheating resume` and `PCell Ul trigger buffer split`.
\* `psPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplit` is called with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes >0` and `initialSplitTxPower`.
\* `start UL schedluing` is initiated with `scell splitTxPower = scell initial SplitTxPower`.
The diagram also includes a footer with the text "http:/msc-generator.sourceforge.net v3.3.7".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3517.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
[CB006137-BB]
case5: scell overheating resume
[End CB006137-BB]
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1812\_UL Initial Split TxPower For Inter-L2PS UL CA.signalling"

MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1834\_UL Power Increase For Inter-L2PS UL CA:
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating power adjustments in a gNB (Next Generation NodeB) DU (Distributed Unit). The diagram depicts interactions between PCell (Primary Cell) and SCell (Secondary Cell) components, specifically their L2RT (Layer 2 Receive/Transmit) functionalities.
The diagram is divided into two main sections, each initiated by an "opt" (optional) trigger: "power increase from Pcell" and "power increase from Scell".
**Section 1: Power Increase from Pcell**
\* **(1.1) Power increase from Pcell in ul overlap slot (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10881):** This indicates a power increase event originating from the Pcell in an uplink overlap slot, identified by a specific algorithm ID.
\* **(1.1.1) pcell splitTxPower += powerAdjustStep:** This message shows that the `pcell splitTxPower` variable is incremented by `powerAdjustStep`.
\* \*\* (1.2) psPeerCtrl\_PcellUIPower Ctrll nd with pcellIncreasingPower: **This represents a control message from `psPeerCtrl` to `PcellUI` related to power control, specifically with `pcellIncreasingPower`.
\* \*\* (1.3) Scell splitTxPower -= pcellIncreasing Power if needed:** This message indicates that `Scell splitTxPower` is decremented by `pcellIncreasingPower`, conditional on it being needed.
**Section 2: Power Increase from Scell**
\* \*\* (2.1) Power increase from Scell in ul overlap slot (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10881): **Similar to the Pcell section, this signifies a power increase event from the SCell in an uplink overlap slot.
\* \*\* (2.1.1) scell splitTxPower += powerAdjustStep:** This message shows that the `scell splitTxPower` variable is incremented by `powerAdjustStep`.
\* \*\* (2.2) psPeerCtrl\_ScellUIHousekeepingReportind with scelllncreasingPower: **This represents a housekeeping report from `psPeerCtrl` to `ScellUI`, related to `scelllncreasingPower`.
\* \*\* (2.3) Pcell splitTxPower -= scelllncreasing Power if needed:** This message indicates that `Pcell splitTxPower` is decremented by `scelllncreasingPower`, conditional on it being needed.
At the top of the diagram, there are labels for `gNB_DU`, `PCell_L2RT`, and `SCell_L2RT`, with sub-components `PCell_DL`, `PCell_UL`, `SCell_UL`, and `SCell_DL` within the respective L2RT boxes.
The bottom right corner contains a URL: `http://mse-generator.sourceforge.net v3.7`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3569.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1834\_UL Power Increase For Inter-L2PS UL CA.signalling"

**8.3.2.5.3.0-2.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11202400`)

Adjust split TX power
For a UE configured with FR1 UL CA, if one Ul scheduling on any cell in an Ul overlapping slot requires more power than the given split power, then adjust split TX power between Pcell and Scell should do.
