Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1842\_UL TX power split with UL bufferSplit For FR1 Inter-L2PS UL CA:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the UL TX power split with UL bufferSplit for FR1 Inter-L2PS UL CA. The diagram depicts interactions between different components: PCell\_DL, PCell\_L2RT, PCell\_UL, SCell\_DL, SCell\_L2RT, SCell\_UL, and Timer.
The diagram is divided into several sections, each representing a specific scenario or condition.
**Pre-condition:**
\* DL-UL SCell activated.
\* UL power split and UL buffer split is running.
**Main Flow (Alt#1):**
This section details the process when the `rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower` timer starts.
1. **PCell\_UL** detects a buffer split stop.
2. **SCell\_DL** receives a `psPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplit` message with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes = 0`.
3. The `rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower` timer starts.
4. **PCell\_UL** continues with the existing splitTxPower in the overlap slot.
5. **SCell\_UL** performs cleanup housekeeping: stops new initial transmission and keeps the existed splitTxPower for retransmission.
**Optional Flow (opt): Buffer split restart within timer:**
This sub-flow occurs if the buffer split restarts while the timer is active.
6. The `rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower` timer is killed.
\* **PCell\_UL** receives a `psPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplit` message with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes != 0`.
\* **PCell\_UL** continues with the existing splitTxPower in the overlap slot.
\* **SCell\_UL** updates housekeeping: starts new initial transmission and continues UL scheduling with the existed splitTxPower.
7. The timer expires.
\* **PCell\_UL** starts scheduling in the overlapping slot with `splitTxPower = servingcellPcmax`.
\* **SCell\_UL** stops scheduling silently.
**Optional Flow (opt): Buffer split restart after timer:**
This sub-flow occurs if the buffer split restarts after the timer has expired.
8. **PCell\_UL** starts buffer split to SCell.
\* **PCell\_UL** starts power split to SCell and UL scheduling in the overlapping slot with `splitTxPower = pcell initialSplitTxPower`.
\* **SCell\_DL** receives a `psPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplit` message with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes != 0 && scell initialSplitTxPower`.
\* **SCell\_UL** starts UL scheduling in the overlapping slot with `scell splitTxPower = scell initialSplitTxPower`.
**Alternative Flow (Alt#2):**
This section details the process when the `rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower` timer does not start.
9. **PCell\_UL** detects a buffer split stop.
10. **SCell\_DL** receives a `psPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplit` message with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes = 0` and `ifHarqNeedClear = true`.
11. **SCell\_UL** stops UL new transmission and re-transmission, and releases the HARQ process.
12. **PCell\_UL** continues UL scheduling with full splitTxPower in the overlapping slot.
The diagram also includes a footer with a URL: `http://www.generator.sourceforge.net v7.2`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3592.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1842\_UL TX power split with bufferSplit For Inter-L2PS UL CA.signalling"

##### 8.3.2.5.4.0-2 Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped Description: (ID: 11202536)

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202542`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(1)(2)(3) buffer split stopped on Pcell

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11202550`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(1)(2):when UE transmission buffer split is stopped, Pcell send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd msg with psPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplit = 0 to Scell.

(3): If buffer split stop triggered except by scell release and scell change, start rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower if the timer is not running,

If buffer split stop triggered by scell release or scell change, stop rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower if the timer is running.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11202557`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(4) UL scheduling and power adjustment stopped on Pcell

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202563`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(4): pcell continue UL scheduling in overlap slot with the splitTxPower before rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower timeout, and can not do power adjustment to avoid enter scell suspend scenario.

Notes:

If bufferSplit stop triggered by scell release and scell change, Pcell splitTxPower should be set to servingcellPcmax, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10919\_replaced([11119940](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11202570`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(5) buffer split stop handling on Scell

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11202578`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(5): rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower is started on Pcell, scell has no sense about this timer. but once received rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes = 0 with PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd msg, Scell would clean housekeeping, and do the UL retransmission with the local spliTxPower if needed. if isHarqNeedClear is true in the PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd, there is no need to do the UL retransmission.There would be no new UL transimssion as no buffer in scell, so the scell splitTxPower do not take effect before rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes !=0 triggered again.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11202585`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(6) buffer split restart before rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower timeout

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11202591`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(6.1)(6.2) buffer split restart before rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower timeout

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11202599`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(6.1)(6.2)If buffer split restart before rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower timeout, the timer should be stopped. Pcell send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd msg with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes != 0 to Scell.

refer to  5G\_UP\_ALG\_10946\_replaced([11120029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8V_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11202606`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(6.3) UL scheduling and power adjustment continue on Pcell

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202614`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(6.3): pcell continue UL scheduling in overlap slot with pcell splitTxPower and do power adjustment if needed.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11202621`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(6.4) UL scheduling and power adjustment continue on Scell

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11202628`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(6.4)  Once rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes != 0 with PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd msg received in Scell,  it would do housekeeping update as buffer in scell restored, so the scell splitTxPower and the corresponding adjustment take effect again.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11202636`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(7) rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower expired after buffer split stop

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11202643`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(7.1): If rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower timeout, pcell suspend should be resumed for ul scheduling. No matter pcell suspend or not, set pcell splitTxPower = servingcellPcmax.

(7.2): Since no buffer in scell, scell UL scheduling can not happen before buffer split start again.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11202650`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(8) buffer split start after rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower expired

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11202657`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(8.1)(8.2)(8.3) buffer split start after rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower expired

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11202663`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(8.1)(8.2) If buffer split start after rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower timeout, pcell should do power split as case2 in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10879\_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). pcell should do UL scheduling in the overlap slot with the pcell splitTxPower = pcell initialSplitTxPower instead of servingcellPcmax.

(8.3) Pcell send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd msg with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes != 0 and scell initialSplitTxPower to Scell.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11202670`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(8.4) scell receive buffer split with power split

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202677`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(8.4) Once received the scell initialSplitTxPower(splitTxPower, powerAdjStep) with PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd, Scell store the scell SplitTxPower, powerAdjStep. Scell can start to do UL scheduling and power adjustment again.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11202687`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(9) buffer split stopped in PCell

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11202693`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
This procedure is applicable for the case of PCell Ul buffer split stop triggered by SCell release/SCell change/Overheating.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-8**  (ID: `11202701`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(10) PCell send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd to SCell

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11202708`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
Pcell send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd msg with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes=0 and ifHarqNeedClear=true to notify SCell Ul suspend.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-9**  (ID: `11202715`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(11) SCell UL sheduling suspend

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11202721`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
When SCell received the buffer split stop via PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd, SCell Ul shall stop new Ul transmission and re-transmission, clear HARQ process.

For Overheating case, SCell shall stop the inactivity timer if it's running.

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-10**  (ID: `11202728`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
(12) PCell UL scheduling with full split Tx Power

---

**8.3.2.5.4.0-2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11202736`)

Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped
PCell Ul could continue UL scheduling with full split Tx Power in overlapping slot since SCell suspend.

---

MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1848\_UL Pcell Suspend or Resume For Inter-L2PS UL CA:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a process flow related to PCell and SCell power control in a gNB\_DU (Next Generation NodeB - Distributed Unit). The diagram shows different components like PCell\_DL, PCell\_L2RT, PCell\_UL, SCell\_UL, SCell\_L2RT, and SCell\_DL.
The process is divided into three main sections, indicated by numbered steps:
**Section 1: PCell no split tx power suspend - condition 1**
\* **(1.1)** A condition is met in "5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921", leading to the suspension of PCell in the UL overlap slot.
\* **(1.2)** A message `psPeerCtrl_ScellUIControlInd` with `powerState: Suspend` is sent.
\* **(1.3)** PCell is suspended in the UL overlap slot.
**Section 2: PCell no split tx power suspend - condition 2**
This section is marked with "Alt#2", suggesting an alternative condition for suspension.
\* **(2.1)** The SCell UL PRB (Physical Resource Block) to be scheduled is greater than `maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower`, and the SCell requires more transmit power in slot t-1.
\* **(2.2)** A message `psPeerCtrl_ScellUlHousekeepingReportInd` is sent with `scellIncreasingPower`.
\* **(2.3)** PCell decreases split transmit power in slot t.
\* **Opt/(2.4)** This is an optional step where PCell has insufficient split transmit power for minimal PRB.
\* **(2.4.1)** A message `psPeerCtrl_PcellUIPowerCtrlInd` with `pcellSuspend` is sent.
\* **(2.4.2)** SCell updates `splitTxPower`.
**Section 3: PCell no split tx power resume**
This section is marked with "Opt", indicating it's an optional part of the flow.
\* **(3.1)** PCell resume check passes in `rdNumForMinSplitTxPowerCheck`, and PCell resumes in the UL overlap slot.
\* **(3.2)** A message `psPeerCtrl_ScellUIControlInd` is sent with `powerState: Resume, initialSplitTxPower`.
\* **(3.3)** PCell resumes in the UL overlap slot.
The diagram also includes a footer with the text "http://mse-generator.sourceforge.net v3.7".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3625.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
 
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1848\_UL Power Split Resume or Suspend Pcell For Inter-L2PS UL CA.signalling"

---

##### 8.3.2.5.5.0-2 Pcell Suspend or Pcell Resume Description: (ID: 11202775)

**8.3.2.5.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202780`)

Pcell Suspend or Pcell Resume
(1) Pcell Suspend - condition1

---

**8.3.2.5.5.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11202788`)

Pcell Suspend or Pcell Resume
Pcell suspend of condition1 via psPeerCtrl\_ScellUlControlInd as below:

(1.1): If condition1 pass in scell, pcell suspend in UL overalp slot should be triggered, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(1.2): Scell UL send psPeerCtrl\_ScellUlControlInd to Pcell UL with powerState : Suspend.

(1.3): Once the suspend info received, pcell should set the power state to suspend in UL overlap slots, then Ue will be removed from CS1 list in UL overlap slots until Pcell resume.

---

**8.3.2.5.5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11202796`)

Pcell Suspend or Pcell Resume
(2) Pcell Suspend - condition2

---

**8.3.2.5.5.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202803`)

Pcell Suspend or Pcell Resume
Pcell suspend of condition2 via psPeerCtrl\_PcellUlPowerCtrlInd as below, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

(2.1).  If SCell Ul Prb number to be scheduled exceeds maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower in overlapping slot (t-1), SCell requires more split tx power.

(2.2).  SCell Ul shall send psPeerCtrl\_ScellUlHousekeepingReportInd with scellIncreasingPower to PCell Ul in overlapping slot (t-1).

(2.3).  PCell's splitTxPower decreases the required scellIncreasingPower in slot t that receives the scellIncreasingPower.

(2.4).  PCell will check if the decreased splitTxPower is enough for scheduling the minimal Ul Prb number according to nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB and TPC value to be transmitted if CLPC is enabled in slot t.

(2.4.1). In case PCell has no enough power to schedule minimal Prb number, PCell will notify SCell that PCell will suspend due to no split tx power via psPeerCtrl\_PcellUlPowerCtrlInd with pcellSuspend.

(2.4.2). SCell will adjust its splitTxPower with full split tx power since no need to leave split tx power for PCell in overlapping slot, PCell can continue re-transmission in non-overlapping slot.

Note: PCell condition2 suspend is applicable for both overpower state and non-overpower state.

---

**8.3.2.5.5.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11202812`)

Pcell Suspend or Pcell Resume
(3) Pcell Resume

---

**8.3.2.5.5.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11202818`)

Pcell Suspend or Pcell Resume
Pcell resume via psPeerCtrl\_ScellUlControlInd as below:

(3.1): If resume check pass with rdNumForMinSplitTxPowerCheck in scell, pcell resume in UL overlap slot should be triggered, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10923\_replaced([11119968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(3.2): Scell UL send psPeerCtrl\_ScellUlControlInd to Pcell UL with powerState : Resume, initialSplitTxPower.

(3.3): Pcell UL scheduling resumed in UL overlap slot with the received initialSplitTxPower.

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a process within a gNB\_DU (gNB Distributed Unit). The diagram depicts interactions between different components, specifically PCell\_L2RT (Primary Cell Layer 2 Receiver/Transmitter) and SCell\_L2RT (Secondary Cell Layer 2 Receiver/Transmitter), further broken down into PCell\_DL (Downlink), PCell\_UL (Uplink), SCell\_DL, and SCell\_UL.
The diagram is divided into two main sections, each marked with an "opt" (optional) indicator, suggesting two distinct scenarios or conditional flows.
**Section 1 (Optional):**
\* **Message (1.1):** This message originates from an unspecified source and is directed towards PCell\_L2RT. It describes a condition: "condition 1 in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921 pass, suspend scell with bufferSplit=0 as there are all ul overlap slots in scell".
\* **Message (1.2):** This message is sent from PCell\_L2RT to SCell\_UL. It contains the command "psPeerCtrl\_PcellUIBufferSplit," with the parameter "rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes = 0".
\* **Message (1.3):** This message is sent from SCell\_UL to SCell\_DL. It indicates "scell suspend in all ul overlap slots".
**Section 2 (Optional):**
\* **Message (2.1):** This message originates from an unspecified source and is directed towards PCell\_L2RT. It states: "resume check pass with rdNumForMinSplitTxPowerCheck, resume scell UL scheduling in ul overlap slots".
\* **Message (2.2):** This message is sent from PCell\_L2RT to SCell\_UL. It contains the command "psPeerCtrl\_PcellUIBufferSplit," with the parameter "rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes != 0, scell initialSplitTxPower".
\* **Message (2.3):** This message is sent from SCell\_UL to SCell\_DL. It indicates "scell resume in all ul overlap slots, scell splitTxPower = initialSplitTxPower".

##### 8.3.2.5.6.0-2 Scell Suspend or Scell Resume Description: (ID: 11202858)

**8.3.2.5.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202864`)

Scell Suspend or Scell Resume
Scell Suspend - condition1

---

**8.3.2.5.6.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11202871`)

Scell Suspend or Scell Resume
Scell suspend of codition1 via psPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd as below:

(1.1): If condition1 pass in pcell, scell suspend in UL overlap slot should be triggered, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(1.2): Pcell UL would start rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower, and send psPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplit to Scell UL with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes = 0.

(1.3): Once Scell receive the rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes = 0, there will be no new UL transmission in overlap slot as no buffer in scell, but retransmission can be continued if needed.

---

**8.3.2.5.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11202877`)

Scell Suspend or Scell Resume
Scell resume

---

**8.3.2.5.6.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202883`)

Scell Suspend or Scell Resume
Scell resume via psPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd as below:

(2.1): If resume check pass with rdNumForMinSplitTxPowerCheck in Pcell, Scell resume in UL overlap slot should be triggered with case2 initialSplitTxPower, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10923\_replaced([11119968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(2.2): Pcell UL send psPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplit != 0 to Scell UL with scell initialSplitTxPower.

(2.3): Scell UL scheduling resumed in UL overlap slot with scell splitTxPower = scell initialSplitTxPower.

Note:

scell resume check should be started after rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower timeout, and check sfn/slot in ue distribution table refer to 5G\_L2\_9227\_replaced([11161975](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25dsqfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 8.3.2.6.0-2 UL CA PHR Forwording Between inter L2-PS Description: (ID: 11202946)

**8.3.2.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202952`)

UL CA PHR Forwording Between inter L2-PS
(1)(3)Check up to date PHR

---

**8.3.2.6.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11202959`)

UL CA PHR Forwording Between inter L2-PS
Validate if the PHR is up to date comparing to the last one. The time for validation includes hyper system frame number, system frame number and slot.

---

**8.3.2.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11202966`)

UL CA PHR Forwording Between inter L2-PS
(2)(4)Apply PHR

---

**8.3.2.6.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11202972`)

UL CA PHR Forwording Between inter L2-PS
Use PHR from peer CC .

---

**8.3.2.6.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11202979`)

UL CA PHR Forwording Between inter L2-PS
(5)(6)(7)(8) Calculate nonPowerLimitedTxPowePerPRB

---

**8.3.2.6.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11202986`)

UL CA PHR Forwording Between inter L2-PS
For a CA UE with FR1 UL Scell configurated, nonPowerLimitedTxPowePerPRB is calculated in each serving Cell. After receiving valid PHR or vPHR directly from L2-LO or peer servingCell, nonPowerLimitedTxPowePerPRB should be calculated.

For the calculation, refer to 5G\_L2\_8660\_replaced([11161551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25b3cfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))..

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "DRX inactivity timer state sync procedure (FR1 Inter L2-RT CA)". The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities, specifically PCell (Primary Cell) and SCell (Secondary Cell) components within a gNB (Next Generation NodeB) Distributed Unit (DU). The entities involved are:
\* **PCell UL 5G-L2PS**
\* **PCell DL 5G-L2PS**
\* **SCell DL 5G-L2PS**
\* **SCell UL 5G-L2PS**
\* **SCell DL only 5G-L2PS**
The diagram shows messages exchanged between these entities, indicated by arrows. Each message is labeled with a number and a description of the action or status update.
Here's a breakdown of the interactions:
1. **Initial State Change:**
\* **(1) $CELL sy no local state change to PCELL DL scheduler:** This message originates from an unspecified source and indicates a local state change for the PCell DL scheduler.
2. **SCell Local State Change:**
\* **(2) SCELL local overall state changed due to: a. local UL state change indicated by intra update or b. local DL state change:** This message is sent from SCell DL 5G-L2PS to PCell DL 5G-L2PS, indicating a change in the SCell's local overall state due to either a local UL state change or a local DL state change.
\* **(2) SCELL local overall state changed due to: a. local DL state change:** This message is sent from SCell DL only 5G-L2PS to PCell DL 5G-L2PS, indicating a change in the SCell's local overall state due to a local DL state change.
3. **Inactivity Timer Status Indication:**
\* **(3) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellDrxInactivityTimerStatusInd:** This message is sent from SCell DL 5G-L2PS and SCell UL 5G-L2PS to PCell DL 5G-L2PS, indicating the status of the DRX inactivity timer for the SCell.
4. **Remote SCELL State Updates:**
\* **(4) update single remote SCELL state:** This message is sent from PCell DL 5G-L2PS to SCell DL 5G-L2PS and SCell UL 5G-L2PS, indicating an update to the state of a single remote SCell.
\* **(4) Remote SCELL overall state changed due to: a. single remote SCELL state change indication:** This message is sent from SCell DL 5G-L2PS to PCell DL 5G-L2PS, indicating that the remote SCell's overall state has changed due to an indication of a single remote SCell state change.
\* **(5) update remote SCELL overall state:** This message is sent from SCell DL 5G-L2PS to PCell DL 5G-L2PS, indicating an update to the remote SCell's overall state.
5. **Internal Scheduler Updates:**
\* **(6) PsInternal\_DITOU IIntra SchedUpdate:** This message is sent from SCell DL 5G-L2PS to PCell DL 5G-L2PS, indicating an internal update to the scheduler.
\* **(6) PsInternal\_UITODIIntraSchedUpdate:** This message is sent from SCell UL 5G-L2PS to PCell DL 5G-L2PS, indicating an internal update to the scheduler.
6. **PCell Broadcast and SCell State Change:**
\* **(7) PCELL broadcast overall state change to SCELL DL and UL scheduler:** This message is sent from PCell DL 5G-L2PS to SCell DL 5G-L2PS and SCell UL 5G-L2PS, broadcasting the PCell's overall state change to the SCell schedulers.
7. **PCell Overall State Change and Status Indication:**
\* **(8) PCELL overall state changed due to: a. local DL state change or b. local UL state change indicated by intra update or c. remote SCELL overall state change:** This message is sent from PCell DL 5G-L2PS to SCell DL 5G-L2PS and SCell UL 5G-L2PS, indicating that the PCell's overall state has changed due to various reasons.
\* **(9) PsPeerCtrl\_PcellStatusInd:** This message is sent from SCell DL 5G-L2PS and SCell UL 5G-L2PS to PCell UL 5G-L2PS, indicating the status of the PCell.
8. **Remote SCELL State Updates (again):**
\* **(10) update remote SCELL overall state:** This message is sent from SCell DL 5G-L2PS and SCell UL 5G-L2PS to PCell UL 5G-L2PS, indicating an update to the remote SCell's overall state.

#### 8.3.2.7.0-2 FR1 CA DRX inactivity timer sync procedure Description: (ID: 11203019)

**8.3.2.7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203026`)

FR1 CA DRX inactivity timer sync procedure
(1) SCell sync local state change to PCELL DL scheduler

---

**8.3.2.7.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11203033`)

FR1 CA DRX inactivity timer sync procedure
SCell shall maintain it's local DRX inactivity timer according to SCELL scheduled grant and proved grant. SCell shall notify it's loca DRX inactivity timer state change to PCell DL scheduler. Detail refer to 5G\_L2\_8381\_replaced([11156653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25BAsvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.2.7.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11203041`)

FR1 CA DRX inactivity timer sync procedure
(2) SCell local inactivityTimer state change

---

**8.3.2.7.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203048`)

FR1 CA DRX inactivity timer sync procedure
SCell local DRX inactivityTimer status should be maintained according to DL and UL scheduling result refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2267\_replaced([11114433](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpkqNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For DL only SCell, DRX inactivityTimer state in UL scheduler is always OFF.

---

**8.3.2.7.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11203055`)

FR1 CA DRX inactivity timer sync procedure
(3) SCell send PsPeerCtrl\_ScellDrxInactivityTimerStatusInd to PCell

---

**8.3.2.7.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11203063`)

FR1 CA DRX inactivity timer sync procedure
SCell DL scheduler shall notify it's local DRX inacvitityTimer state change to PCell DL scheduler by message PsPeerCtrl\_ScellDrxInactivityTimerStatusInd defined in 5G\_L2\_IF\_2774\_replaced([10980770](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VlF2Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

(4-6) PCell update remote SCELL inactivityTimer state

---

**8.3.2.7.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11203077`)

FR1 CA DRX inactivity timer sync procedure
Refer to 5G\_L2\_8421\_replaced([11156499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24_ymfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2014\_replaced([11203140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bgbys_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) SCell UL Suspend or Deactivate Procedure For Inter-L2PS UL CA:
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "SCell UL RLQ Suspend or Deactivate Procedure". The diagram depicts interactions between different network components: gNB\_DU, PCELL\_DL, PCELL\_L2RT, PCELL\_UL, SCELL\_L2RT, and SCELL\_DL.
The procedure begins with the UE in service, SCell added and activated. The diagram then outlines several conditional paths (opt) and loops.
**Key interactions and steps include:**
\* **Loop (1) Checking slot for UE(s) in Ue Group:** This loop initiates the process of checking slots for UEs.
\* **opt (1.1) RLQ evaluation checking pass:** If the RLQ evaluation passes:
\* (1.1.1) The RLQ check number is increased.
\* **opt (1.1.2) Scaled MCS below threshold:** If the scaled MCS is below the threshold:
\* The bad RLQ sample number is increased.
\* Instant DI pathloss is stored.
\* Filtered DI pathloss is calculated and stored.
\* **opt (1.2) Reach the maximum RLQ samples:** If the maximum RLQ samples are reached:
\* (1.2.1) RLQ status is calculated based on bad MCS samples.
\* (1.2.2) The bad RLQ suspend counter is increased.
\* (1.2.3) `rrmSamplesScellBadRLQinUL` and `rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL` are reset.
\* **opt (2) UL RLQ status is bad:** If the UL RLQ status is bad:
\* (2.1) `rlqStatus` is stored as "bad" in SCell UI Ue DB.
\* (2.2) `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUIControllnd` is called with `riqStatus="bad"`.
\* (2.3) `riqStatus` is stored as "bad" in PCell UI Ue DB.
\* (2.4) `Start SCell UI RLQ resume procedure` is initiated.
\* (2.5) PCell Ul stops buffer split, referencing `<5G_L1L2_FLOW_1840>`.
\* (2.6) `PsPeerCtrl_Pcell UIBufferSplitind` is called with `rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes=0`.
\* (2.7) PCell starts a timer for reinitializing Tx Power.
\* (2.8) SCell performs clean housekeeping, stops new transmission, and can continue re-transmission with existing split Tx Power.
\* (2.9) `Start sCellDeactivationTimer GNB timer` is initiated.
\* **opt (2.10) SCell deactivated due to DI&UI inactivity timer expired:** If the SCell is deactivated due to DI&UI inactivity timer expiration:
\* (2.10.1) `SCell deactivation procedure` is executed, referencing `<5G_L1L2_FLOW_1285>`.
\* (2.10.2) A prohibit timer is started for bad RLQ to control new UI activation requests.
\* (2.10.3) UI buffer-based activation occurs after the prohibit timer stops, referencing `<5G_L1L2_FLOW_1280>`.
The diagram also includes a URL at the bottom: `http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v7.2`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3674.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2014\_SCell UL RLQ Suspend or Deactivate Procedure.signalling":

##### 8.3.2.8.1.0-2 SCell scheduling suspend or deactivate procedure Description: (ID: 11203147)

**8.3.2.8.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203155`)

SCell scheduling suspend or deactivate procedure
(1) Periodic Monitoring of Channel Quality in Scell

---

**8.3.2.8.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11203165`)

SCell scheduling suspend or deactivate procedure
When SCell activated, the CA UE will be added to UE distribution table in SCell. In each slot, the UEs in the UE group corresponding to the slot will be evaluated for the RLQ status.

(1.1) For each checking slot, extract UEs from the UE group of UE distribution table and start Ul RLQ evaluation. If evaluation condition checking pass(refer to 5G\_L2\_9070\_replaced([11159478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25RfYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then evaluation algorithm shall be run.

(1.1.1) Update RLQ check sample number: rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL++

(1.1.2) In case the scaledMCS is below the RLQ MCS threshold, then accumulate the bad RLQ sample numer, rrmSamplesScellBadRLQinUL++. The instant and filtered Dl pathloss shall be calculated according to PHR info.

(1.2) When the RLQ check sample number reach the maximum according to sCellChannelEstimationPeriod:

(1.2.1) Calculate the RLQ status according to the percent of bad RLQ sample in all RLQ check sample based on the sCellBadChannelEstimationPercent.

(1.2.2) If RLQ status is bad, increase the bad RLQ suspend counter.

(1.2.3) Reset the rrmNumMcsCheckForRLQinUL and rrmSamplesScellBadRLQinUL.

---

**8.3.2.8.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11203173`)

SCell scheduling suspend or deactivate procedure
(2) SCell Ul RLQ status evaluation is bad

---

**8.3.2.8.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203181`)

SCell scheduling suspend or deactivate procedure
(2.1) SCell Ul shall store the SCell Ul RLQ status in Ue DB, which will be used for RLQ condition check.

(2.2) SCell Ul will notify PCell Ul about the Ul RLQ status via PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUlControlInd.

(2.3) PCell Ul should store this RLQ status in PCell Ul Ue DB, which will be used for buffer split check and start a prohibit timer in case SCell deactivated.

(2.4) SCell Ul shall start Ul RLQ resume procedure according to Dl pathloss, refer to 5G\_L2\_9112\_replaced([11159518](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25RfZ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11889\_replaced([11121652](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwqvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(2.5) PCell Ul will trigger buffer split stop procedure, refer to 5G\_L2\_7784\_replaced([11161228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25aCSfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). And adjust the split tx power accordingly, refer to 5G\_L2\_8639\_replaced([11161904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25dFnPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For the flow, refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1840\_replaced([11202508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgYIZ_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(2.6) PCell Ul stop buffer split by sending PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes = 0 to SCell Ul.

(2.7) PCell Ul shall start rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10946\_replaced([11120029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8V_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), this timer protects the possible Ul re-transmission in SCell, the flow can refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1840\_replaced([11202508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgYIZ_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(2.8) When SCell receives PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes = 0, SCell Ul will clean housekeeping and stop the new Ul transmission, but Ul re-transmission could continue with the existing splitTxPower.

(2.9) SCell Ul shall start inactivity timer.

(2.10) SCell deactivated due to DL&UL inactivity timer expired:

- (2.10.1) When both Dl and Ul inactivity timer expired, SCell will trigger deactivation procedure, refer to joint Dl and Ul SCell deactivation flow: 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1285\_replaced([11201304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgRao_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- (2.10.2) For SCell deactivation with Ul bad RLQ status, PCell Ul will start a prohibit timer to prevent frequent ping-pong between deactivation and activation, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12739\_replaced([11121204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWtVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- (2.10.3) Only after the prohibit timer expired, then PCell Ul will clear Ul RLQ status, and start PCell Ul buffer evaluation check, for joint Dl and Ul SCell buffer based activation procedure refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1280\_replaced([11201049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgPlffvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2015\_replaced([11203214](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bgbyw_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) SCell UL Resume Procedure For Inter-L2PS UL CA:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "SCell UL RLQ Resume Procedure". The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities: gNB\_DU, PCELL\_L2RT, PCELL\_DL, PCELL\_UL, SCELL\_L2RT, SCELL\_UL, and SCELL\_DL.
The procedure starts with "SCell UL scheduling suspend due to bad RLQ status".
The main flow involves several steps:
1. **PCell forward SCell's PHR to SCell periodically**: This is a periodic action.
2. **PsPeerCtrl\_PcellU IPhrForwardind with uePhrForward Info**: This message is sent from PCELL\_DL to PCELL\_UL.
3. **Calculate SCell's instant DI pathloss based on forwarded PHR**: This is an internal calculation within PCELL\_UL.
4. **Check instant and filtered DI pathloss**: Another internal check within PCELL\_UL.
5. **Record consecutive successful resume check number**: This is an internal action within PCELL\_UL.
Following these initial steps, there's a conditional block labeled "Opt (6) n times consecutive DI pathloss checking pass". Inside this block:
\* **(6.1) Change riq Status to good and store in SCell UI Ue DB**: This action is performed by SCELL\_UL.
\* **(6.2) Ps PeerCtrl\_ScellUIControlind riq Status="good"**: This message is sent from SCELL\_UL to PCELL\_UL.
\* **(6.3) Store riqStatus = "good" in PCell UI Ue DB**: This action is performed by PCELL\_UL.
\* **(6.4) Stop RLQ resume check procedure**: This action is performed by PCELL\_UL.
\* **(6.5) SCell UI RLQ resume trigger buffer split**: This action is performed by SCELL\_UL.
The diagram then branches into two main alternatives, "Alt#1" and "Alt#2", based on the state of "rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower".
**Alt#1 (6.6) rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower not expired**:
This alternative further splits into "Opt-1" and "Opt-2".
\* **Opt-1 (6.6.1) PCell Ul buffer enough for split**:
\* **(6.6.1.1) PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUIBufferSplitind with rrmBuffered DataUI TotalBytes>0**: This message is sent from PCELL\_UL to SCELL\_UL.
\* **(6.6.1.2) Stop rd TimerForReinitSplit TxPower**: This action is performed by PCELL\_UL.
\* **(6.6.1.3) Resume SCell Ulscheduling based on existing splitTxPower before RLQ suspend**: This action is performed by SCELL\_UL.
\* **Opt-2 (6.6.2) PCell Ul buffer not enough for split**:
\* **(6.6.2.1) No need to send PsPeerCtrl\_PcelIUIBufferSplitind with rrmBufferedDataU ITotalBytes=0**: This is an internal condition within PCELL\_UL.
\* **(6.6.2.2) Wait for next PCell BSR to trigger buffer split**: This is an internal action within PCELL\_UL.
**Alt#2 (6.7) rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower expired**:
This alternative also splits into "Opt-1" and "Opt-2".
\* **Opt-1 (6.7.1) PCell UI buffer enough for split**:
\* **(6.7.1.1) PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUIBufferSplitind with rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes>0 and initialSplitTxPower**: This message is sent from PCELL\_UL to SCELL\_UL.
\* **(6.7.1.2) Resume SCell Ulscheduling based on split buffer and splitTxPower**: This action is performed by SCELL\_UL.
\* **Opt-2 (6.7.2) PCell UI buffer not enough for split**:
\* **(6.7.2.1) No need to send PsPeerCtrl\_PcelIUIBufferSplitind with rrmBufferedDataU IT otalBytes=0**: This is an internal condition within PCELL\_UL.
\* **(6.7.2.2) Wait for next PCell BSR to trigger initial buffer split and power split**: This is an internal action within PCELL\_UL.
The diagram concludes with a URL at the bottom: "http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v7.2".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3682.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

##### 8.3.2.8.2.0-2 SCell scheduling resume procedure Description: (ID: 11203221)

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203228`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
(1) PCell Ul forward PHR info to SCell

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11203235`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
PCell Ul may receive PHR report including SCell PHR periodically, then it will forward to SCell Ul.

In case SCell has suspended scheduling due to bad RLQ status, only virtual PHR forwarded to SCell.

When SCell scheduling is working during Ul RLQ evaluation, SCell may receive real or virtual forwarded PHR.

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11203245`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
(2) PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlPhrForwardInd

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203253`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
PCell Ul notify SCell Ul PHR info via PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlPhrForwardInd.

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11203260`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
(3) Calculate Dl pathloss

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11203269`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
SCell Ul calculate instant Dl pathloss, in case when RLQ status evaluation is in progress, the filtered or average Dl pathloss will be calculated for bad RLQ sample according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13950\_replaced([11121669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If SCell Ul RLQ resume procedure has started, the filtered or average Dl pathloss will not update any more, it will be used for resume check Dl pathloss threshold.

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11203277`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
(4) Compare instant Dl pathloss and Dl pathloss threshold

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11203285`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11889\_replaced([11121652](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwqvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11203292`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
(5) Record consecutive successful resume check number

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11203298`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11889\_replaced([11121652](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwqvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11203310`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
(6) n times consecutive Dl pathloss check pass

---

**8.3.2.8.2.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11203315`)

SCell scheduling resume procedure
Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11889\_replaced([11121652](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwqvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(6.1) Change and store RLQ status in SCell Ul Ue DB.

(6.2) SCell Ul notify PCell Ul RLQ status change via PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUlControlInd with rlqStatus = good.

(6.3) PCell Ul update and store RLQ status in Ue DB.

(6.4) SCell shall stop SCell Ul RLQ resume check procedure.

(6.5) PCell Ul shall trigger Ul buffer split procedure, refer to 5G\_L2\_7625\_replaced([11161003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25YNH_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and tx power split initialized procedure, refer to 5G\_L2\_7106\_replaced([11161721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25b3evvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For the flow, refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1543\_replaced([11201718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgT26vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1809\_replaced([11202020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgVsFPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(6.6) In case Ul RLQ resume before rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower expired:

(6.6.1) If the data in Ul buffer is enough for buffer split:

(6.6.1.1) PCell Ul send the split buffer to SCell Ul via PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes>0, but without initial splitTxPower.

(6.6.1.2) PCell Ul shall stop the rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower.

(6.6.1.3) SCell Ul should resume new Ul scheduling based on the existing splitTxPower before Ul RLQ suspend.

(6.6.2) If the data in Ul buffer is not enough for buffer split:

(6.6.2.1) PCell Ul don't send buffer split info to SCell.

(6.6.2.2) PCell Ul should wait for the next BSR to trigger buffer split. Note: in such case, the housekeeping triggered buffer split should be forbidden, since the SCell Ul scheduling has been suspended before, and in the time of RLQ resume trigger the Ul buffer data volume has been evaluated.

(6.7) In case Ul RLQ resume after rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower expired:

(6.7.1) If the data in Ul buffer is enough for buffer split:

(6.7.1.1) PCell Ul send the split buffer to SCell Ul via PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes>0, and with initial splitTxPower as speficied in the formula for case2 in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10879\_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(6.7.1.2) SCell Ul should resume new Ul scheduling based on the initial splitTxPower.

(6.7.2) If the data in Ul buffer is not enough for buffer split:

(6.7.2.1) PCell Ul don't send buffer split info to SCell.

(6.7.2.2) PCell Ul should wait for the next BSR to trigger buffer split. Note: in such case, the housekeeping triggered buffer split should be forbidden, since the SCell Ul scheduling has been suspended before, and in the time of RLQ resume trigger the Ul buffer data volume has been evaluated.

---

### 8.3.2.9 FR1 UL CA CQI-based Overheating Handling

#### 8.3.2.9.1 SCell Ul Activation Stop and Recover On Dl only SCell's Overheating status change

MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2061\_replaced([11203351](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgcZzvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) SCell UL Activation Stop or Recover on Dl Only SCell's Overheating Status Change Procedure For Inter-L2PS UL CA:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the process of SCell UL Activation Stop and Recovery based on DL Only SCell's overheating status change. The diagram is divided into two main alternatives, Alt#1 and Alt#2, representing the stop and recovery scenarios respectively.
The diagram depicts interactions between different components: PCELL\_L2RT, PCELL\_DL, PCELL\_UL, gNB\_DU, SCELL\_L2RT (Joint DL&UL), SCELL\_UL, SCELL\_DL, and SCELL\_L2RT (DL Only).
**Alt#1: SCell UI Activation Stop**
\* **(1.1)** DL only SCell detects an overheating procedure with CQI=0, indicated by the message `<5G_L1L2_FLOW_355>`. This message is sent from SCELL\_DL to SCELL\_L2RT (DL Only).
\* **(1.2)** A `DIToUlIntraSchedUpdate` message is sent with `overheatingStatus=true`. This message is sent from SCELL\_DL to PCELL\_DL.
\* **(1.3)** PCell UI will store this SCell's overheating status. This is an internal action within PCell.
\* **(1.4)** PCell UI will stop UI buffer evaluation for SCell activation. This is also an internal action within PCell.
**Alt#2: SCell UI Activation Recovery**
\* **(2.1)** DL only SCell detects an overheating resume procedure with CQI>0, indicated by the message `<5G_L1L2_FLOW_370>`. This message is sent from SCELL\_DL to SCELL\_L2RT (DL Only).
\* **(2.2)** A `DIToUlIntraSchedUpdate` message is sent with `overheatingStatus=false`. This message is sent from SCELL\_DL to PCELL\_DL.
\* **(2.3)** PCell UI will store this SCell's overheating status. This is an internal action within PCell.
\* **(2.4)** PCell UI will continue UI buffer evaluation for SCell activation. This is also an internal action within PCell.
The diagram also includes a footer with the text "http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v7.2".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3699.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
 
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2061\_SCell UL Activation On Dl Only SCell's Overheating Change.signalling":

##### 8.3.2.9.1.0-2 SCell Ul Activation Stop and Recover On Dl only SCell's Overheating status change Description: (ID: 11203358)

**8.3.2.9.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203366`)

SCell Ul Activation Stop and Recover On Dl only SCell's Overheating status change
(1) SCell Ul Activation Stop

---

**8.3.2.9.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11203373`)

SCell Ul Activation Stop and Recover On Dl only SCell's Overheating status change
(1.1) Dl only SCell detect overheating status change(CQI=0), and report to PCell Dl via PsPeerCtrl\_ScellStatusInd with overheatingStatus=true, refer to legacy overheating procedure: 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_355\_replaced([11196230](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfzglfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(1.2) PCell Dl will forward the overheating status to PCell Ul via DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=true.

(1.3) PCell Ul will store this overheating status in Ue DB.

(1.4) When any Dl only SCell's overheating status is set as true, then PCell Ul will stop Ul buffer evaluation check.

---

**8.3.2.9.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11203380`)

SCell Ul Activation Stop and Recover On Dl only SCell's Overheating status change
(2) SCell Ul Activation Recovery

---

**8.3.2.9.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203387`)

SCell Ul Activation Stop and Recover On Dl only SCell's Overheating status change
(2.1) Dl only SCell detect overheating status change(CQI>0), and report to PCell Dl via PsPeerCtrl\_ScellStatusInd with overheatingStatus=false, refer to legacy overheating procedure: 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_370\_replaced([11196336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bf0HqPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(2.2) PCell Dl will forward the overheating status to PCell Ul via DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=false.

(2.3) PCell Ul will store this overheating status in Ue DB.

(2.4) If none of Dl only SCell's overheating status is set as true, then PCell Ul could continue Ul buffer evaluation check.

---

MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2069\_replaced([11203414](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgdA1fvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) SCell UL Scheduling Suspend On Joint DL&UL SCell's Overheating Status Detection For Inter-L2PS UL CA:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "SCell UL Scheduling Suspend On Joint DL&UL SCell's Overheating Status Detection" process. The diagram depicts interactions between different components within a gNB\_DU (gNB Distributed Unit).
The main components involved are:
- PCell\_L2RT (Primary Cell Layer 2 Receiver/Transmitter)
- PCell\_DL (Primary Cell Downlink)
- PCell\_UL (Primary Cell Uplink)
- SCELL\_L2RT - (Joint DL&UL) (Secondary Cell Layer 2 Receiver/Transmitter - Joint Downlink & Uplink)
- SCELL\_UL (Secondary Cell Uplink)
- SCELL\_DL (Secondary Cell Downlink)
The sequence of events is as follows:
1. **(1) Joint DL&UL SCell overheating detection procedure(CQI=0) <5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_355>** - This is the initial trigger for the overheating detection procedure.
2. **(2) DITOUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=true** - PCell\_UL sends an update to SCELL\_UL indicating that the overheating status is true.
3. **(3) PCell Ul will store this SCell's overheating status** - PCell\_UL stores the overheating status of the SCell.
4. **(4) DITOUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=true** - SCELL\_UL sends an update to PCell\_UL indicating that the overheating status is true.
5. **(5) Store Overheating status in SCell UI Ue DB** - SCELL\_UL stores the overheating status in its User Equipment (UE) database.
6. **(6) PCell Ul stop buffer split refer to <5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1840>** - PCell\_UL stops buffer splitting, referencing a specific flow.
7. **(7) PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUIBufferSplitInd with rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes=0, ifHarqNeedClear=true** - PCell\_UL sends an indication to SCELL\_UL regarding buffer split, with specific parameters set to zero and true.
8. **(8) Stop SCell Ul new transmission and re-transmission** - SCELL\_UL stops new transmissions and re-transmissions.
9. **(9) Release HARQ process and stop SCell Ul inactivity timer** - SCELL\_UL releases the HARQ process and stops its inactivity timer.
10. **(10) PCell could continue Ul scheduling with full split TxPower in overlapping slot** - PCell\_UL can continue its UL scheduling with full transmit power in overlapping slots.
The diagram also includes a URL at the bottom: `http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v7.2`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3707.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2069\_SCell UL Scheduling Suspend On Joint DL&UL SCell's Overheating Status Detection.signalling":

---

##### 8.3.2.9.2.0-2 SCell Ul Scheduling Suspend On Joint Dl&amp;Ul SCell's Overheating Status Detection Description: (ID: 11203425)

**8.3.2.9.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203432`)

SCell Ul Scheduling Suspend On Joint Dl&Ul SCell's Overheating Status Detection
SCell Ul Scheduling Suspend

---

**8.3.2.9.2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11203440`)

SCell Ul Scheduling Suspend On Joint Dl&Ul SCell's Overheating Status Detection
(1) Dl only SCell detect overheating status change(CQI=0), and report to PCell Dl via PsPeerCtrl\_ScellStatusInd with overheatingStatus=true, refer to legacy overheating procedure: 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_355\_replaced([11196230](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfzglfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(2) PCell Dl will forward the overheating status to PCell Ul via DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=true.

(3) PCell Ul will store this overheating status in Ue DB.

(4) SCell Dl will forward the overheating status to SCell Ul via DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=true.

(5) SCell Ul should store the overheating status in SCell Ul Ue DB.

(6) When joint Dl&Ul SCell's overheating status is set as true, then PCell Ul will stop Ul buffer split refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1543\_replaced([11201718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgT26vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and adjust split tx power refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1840\_replaced([11202508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgYIZ_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PCell could use full tx power in next overlapping slot.

(7) PCell Ul send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd to SCell Ul with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes=0 and ifHarqNeedClear=true.

(8) SCell Ul shall stop new Ul transmission and re-transmission after receive rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes=0 via PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd.

(9) SCell Ul shall release HARQ process and stop Ul inactivity timer.

(10) PCell Ul could continue Ul scheduling with full splitTxPower in overlapping slot, since there's no power reserved for SCell Ul re-transmission any more.

Note: if PCell Ul has been suspended due to no split Tx Power, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then PCell could resume Ul scheduling in Ul overlapping slot with full split Tx Power.

---

MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2077\_replaced([11203469](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgdA3PvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) SCell UL Scheduling Resume On Joint DL&UL SCell's Overheating Status Recovery For Inter-L2PS UL CA:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "SCell UL Scheduling Resume On Joint DL&UL SCell's Overheating Status Recovery" process. The diagram depicts interactions between different components within the gNB\_DU (gNB Distributed Unit), specifically PCELL\_DL, PCELL\_UL, SCELL\_UL, and SCELL\_DL, as well as a higher-level component SCELL\_L2RT (Joint DL&UL).
The diagram outlines a recovery procedure triggered by an overheating status in an SCell. It shows a sequence of messages and actions exchanged between these components. The process involves updating the overheating status, storing this status, starting timers, and then making decisions based on the PCell's buffer status to either resume SCell UL scheduling or wait for further events.
There are two main options presented: Opt-1, where the PCell buffer is sufficient for a split, and Opt-2, where it is not.
The text within the diagram is as follows:
**Title:** SCell UL Scheduling Resume On Joint DL&UL SCell's Overheating Status Recovery
**Components:**
\* gNB\_DU
\* PCELL\_L2RT
\* PCELL\_DL
\* PCELL\_UL
\* SCELL\_L2RT - (Joint DL&UL)
\* SCELL\_UL
\* SCELL\_DL
**Messages and Actions:**
1. **(1) Joint DL&UL SCell overheating recovery procedure(CQI>0)**
\* `<5G_L1L2_FLOW_370>`
2. **(2) DITOUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=false** (Arrow from PCELL\_UL to SCELL\_UL)
3. **(3) PCell Ul will store this SCell's overheating status** (Action within PCELL\_UL)
4. **(4) DITOUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=false** (Arrow from SCELL\_UL to PCELL\_UL)
5. **(5) Store Overheating status in SCell UI Ue DB** (Action within SCELL\_UL)
6. **(6) SCell Ul start inactivity timer** (Action within SCELL\_UL)
7. **(7) SCell overheating resume trigger PCell Ul buffer split** (Arrow from SCELL\_UL to PCELL\_UL)
**Options:**
\* **Opt-1**
\* **(8) PCell Ul buffer enough for split**
\* **(8.1) PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUIBufferSplitInd with rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes>0 and initialSplitTxPower** (Arrow from PCELL\_UL to SCELL\_UL)
\* **(8.2) Resume SCell Ul scheduling based on SCell splitBuffer and splitTxPower** (Action within SCELL\_UL)
\* **Opt-2**
\* **(9) PCell Ul buffer not enough for split**
\* **(9.1) No need to send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUIBufferSplitInd with rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes=0** (Action within PCELL\_UL)
\* **(9.2) Wait for next PCell BSR to trigger initial splitBuffer and splitTxPower** (Action within PCELL\_UL)
**Footer:** http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v7.2[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3713.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2077\_SCell UL Scheduling Resume On Joint DL&UL SCell's Overheating Status Recovery.signalling":

##### 8.3.2.9.3.0-2 SCell Ul Scheduling Resume On Joint Dl&amp;Ul SCell's Overheating Status Recovery Description: (ID: 11203477)

**8.3.2.9.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203483`)

SCell Ul Scheduling Resume On Joint Dl&Ul SCell's Overheating Status Recovery
SCell Ul Scheduling Resume

---

**8.3.2.9.3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11203490`)

SCell Ul Scheduling Resume On Joint Dl&Ul SCell's Overheating Status Recovery
(1) Dl only SCell detect overheating status change(CQI>0), and report to PCell Dl via PsPeerCtrl\_ScellStatusInd with overheatingStatus=false, refer to legacy overheating procedure: 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_370\_replaced([11196336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bf0HqPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(2) PCell Dl will forward the overheating status to PCell Ul via DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=false.

(3) PCell Ul will store this overheating status in Ue DB.

(4) SCell Dl will forward the overheating status to SCell Ul via DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate with overheatingStatus=false.

(5) SCell Ul should store the overheating status in SCell Ul Ue DB.

(6) SCell Ul shall start Ul inactivity timer.

(7) When joint Dl&Ul SCell's overheating status is set as false, then PCell Ul will trigger Ul buffer split procedure refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1543\_replaced([11201718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgT26vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and initialize split tx power refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1840\_replaced([11202508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgYIZ_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(8) If PCell Ul buffer data is enough for buffer split:

(8.1) PCell Ul send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd to SCell Ul with rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes>0 and initialSplitTxPower.

(8.2) SCell Ul shall resume new Ul scheduling based on the initial splitTxPower.

(9) If PCell Ul buffer data is not enough for buffer split:

(9.1) PCell Ul don't send buffer split info to SCell Ul.

(9.2) PCell Ul should wait for the next BSR to trigger buffer split. Note: in such case, the housekeeping triggered buffer split should be forbidden, since the SCell Ul scheduling has been suspended before, and in the time of RLQ resume trigger the Ul buffer data volume has been evaluated.

---

Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_3576\_Sag1x2x4x.signalling" file:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "UL Slot Aggregation (SAG) 1x/2x/4x Repetition Harq Tx" process. The diagram depicts interactions between four entities: UE, 5G-L1-UL, 5G-L1-DL, 5G-L2-PS, and 5G\_L2-LO.
The diagram outlines a process involving data transmission, reception, and HARQ (Hybrid Automatic Repeat Request) retransmissions. Key steps include:
1. **Initial Transmission:**
\* 5G-L1-DL sends a `DIData_PdcchSendReq(DCI:repetition)` to 5G-L2-PS.
\* 5G-L2-PS initiates UL Mac Scheduling.
\* UE receives a `PDCCH` from 5G-L1-UL.
2. **PUSCH Repetitions (Loop):**
\* UE sends `UIData_PuschReceiveReq(RV,CountDown)` to 5G-L1-UL.
\* UE transmits `PUSCH(RV)` to 5G-L1-UL.
\* 5G-L1-UL sends `UIData_PuschReceiveRespPs(CountDown)` to 5G-L2-PS.
\* An optional step depends on whether `HarqAckBits` exist on the current slot.
\* 5G-L2-PS sends `UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD()` and `UIData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU(CRC)` to 5G-L1-DL.
3. **CRC Status Check and Retransmission (Alt):**
\* The process checks the CRC status of the last `HarqU`.
\* **If** the last `HarqU` is `CRC_NOK` and the number of transmissions (`numOfTx`) is less than the maximum allowed (`maxUlHarqNumber`), the process enters a loop for `Harq ReTx of the Whole Repetitions`.
\* Within this retransmission loop, UL Mac Scheduling is performed, and steps (1) to (3) are rerun.
4. **Final Transmission Outcome:**
\* **If** the last `HarqU` is `CRC_NOK` and `numOfTx` equals `maxUlHarqNumber`, `Release Harq` is initiated.
\* **If** the last `HarqU` is `CRC_OK`, UE sends `UIData_PuschReceiveRespLo` to 5G-L1-UL.
The diagram uses standard sequence diagram notation, including lifelines for entities, messages exchanged between them, loops, and alternative flows. The title indicates the context of the diagram is related to uplink slot aggregation with different repetition factors and HARQ transmission.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-03121444.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

---

#### 8.3.3.1.2 Description:

##### 8.3.3.1.2.0-1 Description: (1) DlData_PdcchSendReq (ID: 11203549)

**8.3.3.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11203556`)

Description:
TDRA index in DCI 0\_1 indicates which repetition to be used , refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19266\_replaced([11204842](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4NvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB011118-A] for FDD, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21213\_replaced([11205007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwmfSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for TDD [End CB011118-A] SAg TDRA Tables

Repetitions == n1 (x1) means one PUSCH transmission

Repetitions == n2 (x2) means two successive PUSCH transmissions

[CB011118-A]

For FDD, the Repetitions == n4 (x4) means four sucessive PUSCH transmissions

For TDD, the Repetitions == n12 (x4) means four sucessive PUSCH transmissions

[End CB011118-A]

---

##### 8.3.3.1.2.0-2 Description: (2) PDCCH (ID: 11203563)

**8.3.3.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203570`)

Description:
Refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_561\_replaced([11200624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgNwQPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 8.3.3.1.2.0-3 Description: (3) Loop (ID: 11203578)

**8.3.3.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11203585`)

Description:
Times of loop depend on used repetitions, for CB008236 three repetitions are supported:

1.  1x repetition,  loop once, this is same as legacy pusch transmission, CountDown is always filled with the value 255.

2.  2x repetition,  loop two times, two PUSCH transmissions on successive slots, the first one uses RV=0 and CountDown=1; the second one uses RV=2 and CountDown=0.

3.  4x repetition,  loop four times, four PUSCH transmissions on successive slots, the RV values are 0,2,3,1 separately and CountDown are 3,2,1,0 separately.

How RV is determined, please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19345\_replaced([11205186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwntaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

How CountDown is determined, please refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_191\_replaced([11513756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy99_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_200\_replaced([11513831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD is conditionally presented depending on whether harqBits on specific PUSCH slot exists. It is determined per PUSCH slot.

UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqU feedbacks CRC=OK or CRC=NOK only in the last repetition PUSCH, CRC=INVALID for all other repetition PUSCH. Please refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_209\_replaced([11513897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlD_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 8.3.3.1.2.0-4 Description: (4) the last HarqU==CRC_NOK and numOfTx&lt;maxUlHarqNumber (ID: 11203592)

**8.3.3.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11203600`)

Description:
If harq fails, the whole bundle needs to be re-transmitted.

For 2x or 4x bundle, the maximum number of HARQs(maxUlHarqNumber) is defined by the NIDD parameter maxHarqBundlesUlSlotAgg, please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12741\_replaced([11203324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For 1x, maxUlHarqNumber is same as legacy used maxUlHarqTx, refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_561\_replaced([11200624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgNwQPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.3.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11203617`)

Refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_561\_replaced([11200624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgNwQPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

##### 8.3.3.1.2.0-6 Description: (6) the Last HarqU==CRC_NOK and numOfTx==maxUlHarqNumber (ID: 11203623)

**8.3.3.1.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11203629`)

Description:
maxUlHarqNumber refers to (4)

##### 8.3.3.1.2.0-7 Description: (8) UlData_PuschReceiveRespLo (ID: 11203637)

**8.3.3.1.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11203645`)

Description:
This message is sent only one time regardless of 1x, 2x, or 4x. That means L1 will not send it until all repetitions are received and the combined PUSCH decoding is successful(CRC\_OK).

### 8.3.4.0-1 UL Throughput Counters Creator: Joanna Borkowska (Nokia) Document Owner: Joanna Borkowska (Nokia) (ID: 11203667)

### 8.3.4.1 RLC SDU average uplink throughput

#### 8.3.4.1.1 Call flow:

##### 8.3.4.1.1.0-1 Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: 11203691: Call flow: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the MSC643 RLC average uplink throughput. It depicts the interaction between different components of a 5G network, specifically the gNB DU (gNB Distributed Unit) and the gNB CU (gNB Centralized Unit). The gNB DU is further divided into two logical layers: 5G-L2-LO and 5G-L2-HI DU. The gNB CU has a single logical layer: 5G-L2-HI CU. The diagram shows a sequence of messages exchanged between these components, numbered from (1) to (6). 1. (1) LoData_UeBufferEmptyInd : This message is sent from 5G-L2-LO to 5G-L2-HI DU, indicating that the UE buffer is not empty ( ueBufferEmpty = False ). 2. (2) LoData_RlcPduReceiveInd : This message is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-LO, indicating the reception of an RLC PDU (RLC Protocol Data Unit) named 'n'. 3. (3) RLC SDU n : This message represents an RLC SDU (Service Data Unit) 'n' being sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU. 4. (4) LoData_RlcPduReceiveInd : Similar to (2), this message is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-LO, indicating the reception of another RLC PDU named 'n+1'. 5. (5) RLC SDU n+1 : This message represents an RLC SDU 'n+1' being sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-HI CU. 6. (6) LoData_UeBufferEmptyInd : This message is sent from 5G-L2-HI DU to 5G-L2-LO, indicating that the UE buffer is now empty ( ueBufferEmpty = True ). The diagram also includes a dashed arrow indicating "More RLC PDUs within burst," suggesting that multiple RLC PDUs can be processed in a single burst. The overall context is the average uplink throughput of the RLC layer.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_3743.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link to the "MSC 5G_L1L2_FLOW_643_22R1_RlcAverageUplinkThroughput.signalling" file: (ID: 11203691)

#### 8.3.4.1.2 Description:

**8.3.4.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11203703`)

Description:
(1) LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd

Direction: 5G-L2-LO -> 5G-L2-HI DU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_1539\_replaced([11513127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tT0Imvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.4.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11203710`)

Description:
 At reception of LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd = FALSE, 5G-L2-Hi DU shall start observing the burst.

---

**8.3.4.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `11203717`)

Description:
(2) LoData\_RlcPduReceiveInd

Direction: 5G-L2-LO -> 5G-L2-HI DU

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_940\_replaced([10985934](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WLix_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.4.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203723`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi DU shall receive LoData\_RlcPduReceiveInd from 5G-L2-Lo.

 5G-L2-Hi DU shall update ThpVolDl by the size of received RLC PDU n.

 5G-L2-Hi DU shall process RLC PDU n into RLC SDU n according to 5G\_L2\_2344\_replaced([11224332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_v62PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 5G-L2-Hi DU shall save in tstartOfBurst the time of reception of first RLC PDU.

---

**8.3.4.1.2.0-3**  (ID: `11203731`)

Description:
(3) RLC SDU n

Direction: 5G-L2-HI DU -> 5G-L2-HI CU

Message definition: 5G\_UP\_IF\_3475\_replaced([11530659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWaJnfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.4.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11203738`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi DU shall send RLC SDU n towards 5G-L2-Hi CU according to 5G\_L2\_2344\_replaced([11224332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_v62PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**8.3.4.1.2.0-4**  (ID: `11203743`)

Description:
(4) LoData\_RlcPduReceiveInd

Direction: 5G-L2-LO -> 5G-L2-HI DU

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_940\_replaced([10985934](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WLix_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.4.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11203749`)

Description:
 5G-L2-Hi DU shall receive LoData\_RlcPduReceiveInd from 5G-L2-Lo.

 5G-L2-Hi DU shall update ThpVolDl by the size of received RLC SDU n+1.

 5G-L2-Hi DU shall save the time of reception of the RLC PDU n+1.

 5G-L2-Hi DU shall process RLC PDU n+1 into RLC SDU n+1 according to 5G\_L2\_2344\_replaced([11224332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_v62PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 5G-L2-Hi DU shall save in tEndOfBurst the time of reception of RLC PDU n+1 and calculate the time of burst lasting according to the formula: ThpTimeUl = tEndOfBurst – tStartOfBurst. .

**8.3.4.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11203763`)

**8.3.4.1.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11203777`)

Description:
 At reception of LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd = TRUE,  5G-L2-Hi DU shall stop observing the burst.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "MSC 6311 UL Congestion Information Reporting" process. The diagram depicts interactions between three entities: "Timer", "5G-L2-PS", "5G-L2-LO", and "5G-L2-HI(DU)".
The diagram shows the following sequence of events:
1. **Timer** initiates the process by sending a "start rdL4sUciReportingPeriod" message to **5G-L2-PS**.
2. **5G-L2-PS** receives a "LoCtrl\_UlMacPduReceiveInd" message from **5G-L2-LO**.
3. **5G-L2-PS** optionally receives "A BSR is Received".
4. **5G-L2-PS** optionally calculates "UCI".
5. The "rdL4sUciReportingPeriod" expires.
6. **5G-L2-LO** sends "LoData\_UIRIcPduReceiveInd" to **5G-L2-HI(DU)**.
7. **5G-L2-LO** sends "LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd" to **5G-L2-HI(DU)**.
8. **5G-L2-LO** optionally indicates that "UCI is Available".
9. **5G-L2-LO** sends "LoCtrl\_UciUpdateReq (UCI)" to **5G-L2-PS**.
10. **5G-L2-HI(DU)** optionally receives "LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd (UCI)".
11. **5G-L2-HI(DU)** receives "LoCtrl\_UIMacPduReceiveInd" from **5G-L2-PS**.
12. **5G-L2-HI(DU)** receives "LoData\_UIRIcPduReceiveInd".
13. **5G-L2-HI(DU)** receives "LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd(UCI)".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_3763.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
Link to the "MSC6311\_25R2\_UplinkCongestionInfoReporting.signalling" file:

---

#### 8.3.5.1.2 Description:

**8.3.5.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11203845`)

Description:
(2)(11) LoCtrl\_UlMacPduReceiveInd

Direction: 5G-L2-LO -> 5G-L2-PS

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_875\_replaced([10984687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBxzvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11203853`)

Description:
At reception of the UL data packet from 5G-L2-L1, 5G-L2-LO sends the LoCtrl\_UlMacPduReceiveInd  to 5G-L2-PS

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `11203860`)

Description:
(6)(12) LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd

Direction: 5G-L2-LO -> 5G-L2-HI

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_940\_replaced([10985934](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WLix_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11203865`)

Description:
At reception of the UL data packet from 5G-L2-L1, 5G-L2-LO sends the LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd to 5G-L2-HIDU

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-3**  (ID: `11203872`)

Description:
(7) LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd

Direction: 5G-L2-LO -> 5G-L2-HI

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_1539\_replaced([10986158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WNX8vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11203879`)

Description:
At reception of the UL data packet from 5G-L2-L1, 5G-L2-LO sends the LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd to 5G-L2-HIDU  with ueBufferEmpty=FALSE

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-4**  (ID: `11203886`)

Description:
(9) LoCtrl\_UciUpdateReq

Direction: 5G-L2-PS -> 5G-L2-LO

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_7181\_replaced([10985653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WJtkPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11203893`)

Description:
At reception of the LoCtrl\_UlMacPduReceiveInd from 5G-L2-LO, if l4sAlgorithm is enabled in UL and BSR is received, 5G-L2-PS calculates UCI and after every rdL4sUciReportingPeriod(see 5G\_L2\_2174\_replaced([11221072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_cY1_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ms, if there is UCI availablel then sends the LoCtrl\_UciUpdateReq with list of calculated UCI for each L4S bearer (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28196\_replaced([11203979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwiN2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-5**  (ID: `11203899`)

Description:
(10) LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd

Direction: 5G-L2-LO -> 5G-L2-HI

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_1539\_replaced([10986158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WNX8vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11203906`)

Description:
At reception of the LoCtrl\_UciUpdateReq from 5G-L2-PS, 5G-L2-LO sends the LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd to 5G-L2-HIDU  with UCI received from 5G-L2-PS

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-6**  (ID: `11203913`)

Description:
(13) LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd

Direction: 5G-L2-LO -> 5G-L2-HI

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_1539\_replaced([10986158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WNX8vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**8.3.5.1.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11203921`)

Description:
At reception of the LoCtrl\_UciUpdateReq from 5G-L2-PS, 5G-L2-LO sends the LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd to 5G-L2-HIDU  with UCI received from 5G-L2-PS

---

#### 8.3.5.1.3 Exceptions
